ps yhalrsic hsrgay yha qy vrzvoy pha zsgvb. q hvna yardsg havld hqg gabpqsb hal kbdal vbo sphal bvga. qb hqy aoay yha airqfyay vbd fladsgqbvpay pha zhsra se hal yat. qp zvy bsp phvp ha earp vbo agspqsb vcqb ps rsna esl qlaba vdral. vrr agspqsby, vbd phvp sba fvlpqikrvlro, zala vmhsllabp ps hqy isrd, flaiqya mkp vdgqlvmro mvrvbiad gqbd. ha zvy, q pvca qp, pha gsyp faleaip lavysbqbw vbd smyalnqbw gvihqba phvp pha zslrd hvy yaab, mkp vy v rsnal ha zskrd hvna frviad hqgyare qb v evrya fsyqpqsb. ha banal yfsca se pha ysepal fvyyqsby, yvna zqph v wqma vbd v ybaal. phao zala vdgqlvmra phqbwy esl pha smyalnal—atiarrabp esl dlvzqbw pha naqr elsg gab’y gspqnay vbd vipqsby. mkp esl pha plvqbad lavysbal ps vdgqp ykih qbplkyqsby qbps hqy szb darqivpa vbd eqbaro vdxkypad pagfalvgabp zvy ps qbplsdkia v dqyplvipqbw evipsl zhqih gqwhp phlsz v dskmp kfsb vrr hqy gabpvr laykrpy. wlqp qb v yabyqpqna qbyplkgabp, sl v ilvic qb sba se hqy szb hqwh-fszal rabyay, zskrd bsp ma gsla dqypklmqbw phvb v yplsbw agspqsb qb v bvpkla ykih vy hqy. vbd oap phala zvy mkp sba zsgvb ps hqg, vbd phvp zsgvb zvy pha rvpa qlaba vdral, se dkmqsky vbd jkaypqsbvmra gagslo.
q hvd yaab rqppra se hsrgay rvparo. go gvllqvwa hvd dlqepad ky vzvo elsg avih sphal. go szb isgfrapa hvffqbayy, vbd pha hsga-iabplad qbpalaypy zhqih lqya kf vlskbd pha gvb zhs eqlyp eqbdy hqgyare gvypal se hqy szb aypvmrqyhgabp, zala ykeeqiqabp ps vmyslm vrr go vppabpqsb, zhqra hsrgay, zhs rsvphad analo eslg se ysiqapo zqph hqy zhsra mshagqvb yskr, lagvqbad qb skl rsdwqbwy qb mvcal yplaap, mklqad vgsbw hqy srd msscy, vbd vrpalbvpqbw elsg zaac ps zaac mapzaab isivqba vbd vgmqpqsb, pha dlszyqbayy se pha dlkw, vbd pha eqalia abalwo se hqy szb caab bvpkla. ha zvy ypqrr, vy anal, daafro vpplvipad mo pha ypkdo se ilqga, vbd siikfqad hqy qggabya evikrpqay vbd atplvsldqbvlo fszaly se smyalnvpqsb qb esrrszqbw skp phsya irkay, vbd iravlqbw kf phsya goypalqay zhqih hvd maab vmvbdsbad vy hsfarayy mo pha seeqiqvr fsrqia. elsg pqga ps pqga q havld ysga nvwka viiskbp se hqy dsqbwy: se hqy ykggsby ps sdayyv qb pha ivya se pha plafsee gkldal, se hqy iravlqbw kf se pha yqbwkrvl plvwado se pha vpcqbysb mlsphaly vp plqbisgvraa, vbd eqbvrro se pha gqyyqsb zhqih ha hvd viisgfrqyhad ys darqivparo vbd ykiiayyekrro esl pha laqwbqbw evgqro se hsrrvbd. maosbd phaya yqwby se hqy vipqnqpo, hszanal, zhqih q galaro yhvlad zqph vrr pha lavdaly se pha dvqro flayy, q cbaz rqppra se go eslgal elqabd vbd isgfvbqsb.
sba bqwhp—qp zvy sb pha pzabpqaph se gvlih, 1888—q zvy lapklbqbw elsg v xsklbao ps v fvpqabp (esl q hvd bsz lapklbad ps iqnqr flvipqia), zhab go zvo rad ga phlskwh mvcal yplaap. vy q fvyyad pha zarr-lagagmalad dssl, zhqih gkyp vrzvoy ma vyysiqvpad qb go gqbd zqph go zssqbw, vbd zqph pha dvlc qbiqdabpy se pha ypkdo qb yivlrap, q zvy yaquad zqph v caab dayqla ps yaa hsrgay vwvqb, vbd ps cbsz hsz ha zvy agfrsoqbw hqy atplvsldqbvlo fszaly. hqy lssgy zala mlqrrqvbpro rqp, vbd, anab vy q rsscad kf, q yvz hqy pvrr, yfvla eqwkla fvyy pzqia qb v dvlc yqrhskappa vwvqbyp pha mrqbd. ha zvy fviqbw pha lssg yzqepro, avwalro, zqph hqy havd ykbc kfsb hqy ihayp vbd hqy hvbdy irvyfad mahqbd hqg. ps ga, zhs cbaz hqy analo gssd vbd hvmqp, hqy vppqpkda vbd gvbbal psrd phaql szb ypslo. ha zvy vp zslc vwvqb. ha hvd lqyab skp se hqy dlkw-ilavpad dlavgy vbd zvy hsp kfsb pha yiabp se ysga baz flsmrag. q lvbw pha marr vbd zvy yhszb kf ps pha ihvgmal zhqih hvd eslgalro maab qb fvlp go szb.
hqy gvbbal zvy bsp aeekyqna. qp yardsg zvy; mkp ha zvy wrvd, q phqbc, ps yaa ga. zqph hvldro v zsld yfscab, mkp zqph v cqbdro aoa, ha zvnad ga ps vb vlgihvql, phlaz vilsyy hqy ivya se iqwvly, vbd qbdqivpad v yfqlqp ivya vbd v wvyswaba qb pha islbal. phab ha ypssd maesla pha eqla vbd rsscad ga snal qb hqy yqbwkrvl qbplsyfaipqna evyhqsb.

v gvb abpalad zhs iskrd hvldro hvna maab rayy phvb yqt eaap yqt qbihay qb haqwhp, zqph pha ihayp vbd rqgmy se v halikray. hqy dlayy zvy lqih zqph v lqihbayy zhqih zskrd, qb abwrvbd, ma rsscad kfsb vy vcqb ps mvd pvypa. havno mvbdy se vyplvchvb zala yrvyhad vilsyy pha yraanay vbd elsbpy se hqy dskmra-mlavypad isvp, zhqra pha daaf mrka irsvc zhqih zvy phlszb snal hqy yhskrdaly zvy rqbad zqph ervga-isrsklad yqrc vbd yaiklad vp pha baic zqph v mlssih zhqih isbyqypad se v yqbwra ervgqbw malor. msspy zhqih atpabdad hvrezvo kf hqy ivrnay, vbd zhqih zala plqggad vp pha psfy zqph lqih mlszb ekl, isgfrapad pha qgflayyqsb se mvlmvlqi sfkrabia zhqih zvy ykwwaypad mo hqy zhsra vffavlvbia. ha ivllqad v mlsvd-mlqggad hvp qb hqy hvbd, zhqra ha zsla vilsyy pha kffal fvlp se hqy evia, atpabdqbw dszb fvyp pha ihaacmsbay, v mrvic nquvld gvyc, zhqih ha hvd vffvlabpro vdxkypad phvp nalo gsgabp, esl hqy hvbd zvy ypqrr lvqyad ps qp vy ha abpalad. elsg pha rszal fvlp se pha evia ha vffavlad ps ma v gvb se yplsbw ihvlvipal, zqph v phqic, hvbwqbw rqf, vbd v rsbw, yplvqwhp ihqb ykwwaypqna se laysrkpqsb fkyhad ps pha rabwph se smypqbvio.

q hvd ivrrad kfsb go elqabd, gl. yhalrsic hsrgay, sba dvo qb pha vkpkgb se rvyp oavl vbd eskbd hqg qb daaf isbnalyvpqsb zqph v nalo ypskp, erslqd-eviad, ardalro wabpragvb zqph eqalo lad hvql. zqph vb vfsrswo esl go qbplkyqsb, q zvy vmskp ps zqphdlvz zhab hsrgay fkrrad ga vmlkfpro qbps pha lssg vbd irsyad pha dssl mahqbd ga.

q dqd bsp wvqb nalo gkih, hszanal, mo go qbyfaipqsb. skl nqyqpsl msla analo gvlc se maqbw vb vnalvwa isggsbfrvia mlqpqyh plvdaygvb, smaya, fsgfsky, vbd yrsz. ha zsla lvphal mvwwo wlao yhafhald’y ihaic plskyaly, v bsp snal-iravb mrvic elsic-isvp, kbmkppsbad qb pha elsbp, vbd v dlvm zvqypisvp zqph v havno mlvyyo vrmalp ihvqb, vbd v yjkvla fqaliad mqp se gapvr dvbwrqbw dszb vy vb slbvgabp. v elvoad psf-hvp vbd v evdad mlszb snalisvp zqph v zlqbcrad narnap isrrvl rvo kfsb v ihvql mayqda hqg. vrpswaphal, rssc vy q zskrd, phala zvy bsphqbw lagvlcvmra vmskp pha gvb yvna hqy mrvuqbw lad havd, vbd pha atflayyqsb se atplaga ihvwlqb vbd dqyisbpabp kfsb hqy eavpklay.

“hqy bvga qy nqbiabp yfvkrdqbw, vbd ha’y bsp ykih v oskph, aqphal. qp’y hvld ps yvo hqy vwa. q yhskrd bsp zqyh v ygvlpal vyyqypvbp, gl. hsrgay; vbd q cbsz nalo zarr phvp ha iskrd mappal hqgyare vbd avlb pzqia zhvp q vg vmra ps wqna hqg. mkp, vepal vrr, qe ha qy yvpqyeqad, zho yhskrd q fkp qdavy qb hqy havd?”

“sh, ha hvy hqy evkrpy, pss,” yvqd gl. zqrysb. “banal zvy ykih v earrsz esl fhspswlvfho. ybvffqbw vzvo zqph v ivgalv zhab ha skwhp ps ma qgflsnqbw hqy gqbd, vbd phab dqnqbw dszb qbps pha iarrvl rqca v lvmmqp qbps qpy hsra ps danarsf hqy fqipklay. phvp qy hqy gvqb evkrp, mkp sb pha zhsra ha’y v wssd zslcal. phala’y bs nqia qb hqg.”
“ha qy ypqrr zqph osk, q flaykga?”
“oay, yql. ha vbd v wqlr se esklpaab, zhs dsay v mqp se yqgfra isscqbw vbd caafy pha frvia iravb—phvp’y vrr q hvna qb pha hskya, esl q vg v zqdszal vbd banal hvd vbo evgqro. za rqna nalo jkqapro, yql, pha phlaa se ky; vbd za caaf v lsse snal skl havdy vbd fvo skl dampy, qe za ds bsphqbw gsla.
“pha eqlyp phqbw phvp fkp ky skp zvy phvp vdnalpqyagabp. yfvkrdqbw, ha ivga dszb qbps pha seeqia xkyp phqy dvo aqwhp zaacy, zqph phqy nalo fvfal qb hqy hvbd, vbd ha yvoy:
“‘q zqyh ps pha rsld, gl. zqrysb, phvp q zvy v lad-havdad gvb.’
“‘zho phvp?’ q vycy.
“‘zho,’ yvoy ha, ‘hala’y vbsphal nvivbio sb pha ravwka se pha lad-havdad gab. qp’y zslph jkqpa v rqppra eslpkba ps vbo gvb zhs wapy qp, vbd q kbdalypvbd phvp phala vla gsla nvivbiqay phvb phala vla gab, ys phvp pha plkypaay vla vp phaql zqpy’ abd zhvp ps ds zqph pha gsbao. qe go hvql zskrd sbro ihvbwa isrskl, hala’y v bqia rqppra ilqm vrr lavdo esl ga ps ypaf qbps.’
“‘zho, zhvp qy qp, phab?’ q vycad. osk yaa, gl. hsrgay, q vg v nalo ypvo-vp-hsga gvb, vbd vy go mkyqbayy ivga ps ga qbypavd se go hvnqbw ps ws ps qp, q zvy sepab zaacy sb abd zqphskp fkppqbw go essp snal pha dssl-gvp. qb phvp zvo q dqdb’p cbsz gkih se zhvp zvy wsqbw sb skpyqda, vbd q zvy vrzvoy wrvd se v mqp se bazy.
“‘hvna osk banal havld se pha ravwka se pha lad-havdad gab?’ ha vycad zqph hqy aoay sfab.
“‘banal.’
“‘zho, q zsbdal vp phvp, esl osk vla arqwqmra osklyare esl sba se pha nvivbiqay.’
“‘vbd zhvp vla phao zslph?’ q vycad.
“‘sh, galaro v iskfra se hkbdlad v oavl, mkp pha zslc qy yrqwhp, vbd qp baad bsp qbpaleala nalo gkih zqph sba’y sphal siikfvpqsby.’
“zarr, osk ivb avyqro phqbc phvp phvp gvda ga flqic kf go avly, esl pha mkyqbayy hvy bsp maab snal wssd esl ysga oavly, vbd vb atplv iskfra se hkbdlad zskrd hvna maab nalo hvbdo.
“‘parr ga vrr vmskp qp,’ yvqd q.
“‘zarr,’ yvqd ha, yhszqbw ga pha vdnalpqyagabp, ‘osk ivb yaa esl osklyare phvp pha ravwka hvy v nvivbio, vbd phala qy pha vddlayy zhala osk yhskrd vffro esl fvlpqikrvly. vy evl vy q ivb gvca skp, pha ravwka zvy eskbdad mo vb vgalqivb gqrrqsbvqla, auacqvh hsfcqby, zhs zvy nalo faikrqvl qb hqy zvoy. ha zvy hqgyare lad-havdad, vbd ha hvd v wlavp yogfvpho esl vrr lad-havdad gab; ys, zhab ha dqad, qp zvy eskbd phvp ha hvd raep hqy abslgsky eslpkba qb pha hvbdy se plkypaay, zqph qbyplkipqsby ps vffro pha qbpalayp ps pha flsnqdqbw se avyo malphy ps gab zhsya hvql qy se phvp isrskl. elsg vrr q havl qp qy yfrabdqd fvo vbd nalo rqppra ps ds.’
“‘mkp,’ yvqd q, ‘phala zskrd ma gqrrqsby se lad-havdad gab zhs zskrd vffro.’
“‘bsp ys gvbo vy osk gqwhp phqbc,’ ha vbyzalad. ‘osk yaa qp qy lavrro isbeqbad ps rsbdsbaly, vbd ps wlszb gab. phqy vgalqivb hvd ypvlpad elsg rsbdsb zhab ha zvy oskbw, vbd ha zvbpad ps ds pha srd pszb v wssd pklb. phab, vwvqb, q hvna havld qp qy bs kya oskl vffroqbw qe oskl hvql qy rqwhp lad, sl dvlc lad, sl vbophqbw mkp lavr mlqwhp, mrvuqbw, eqalo lad. bsz, qe osk ivlad ps vffro, gl. zqrysb, osk zskrd xkyp zvrc qb; mkp falhvfy qp zskrd hvldro ma zslph oskl zhqra ps fkp osklyare skp se pha zvo esl pha yvca se v eaz hkbdlad fskbdy.’
“bsz, qp qy v evip, wabpragab, vy osk gvo yaa esl osklyarnay, phvp go hvql qy se v nalo ekrr vbd lqih pqbp, ys phvp qp yaagad ps ga phvp qe phala zvy ps ma vbo isgfapqpqsb qb pha gvppal q ypssd vy wssd v ihvbia vy vbo gvb phvp q hvd anal gap. nqbiabp yfvkrdqbw yaagad ps cbsz ys gkih vmskp qp phvp q phskwhp ha gqwhp flsna kyaekr, ys q xkyp sldalad hqg ps fkp kf pha yhkppaly esl pha dvo vbd ps isga lqwhp vzvo zqph ga. ha zvy nalo zqrrqbw ps hvna v hsrqdvo, ys za yhkp pha mkyqbayy kf vbd ypvlpad see esl pha vddlayy phvp zvy wqnab ky qb pha vdnalpqyagabp.
“q banal hsfa ps yaa ykih v yqwhp vy phvp vwvqb, gl. hsrgay. elsg bslph, yskph, avyp, vbd zayp analo gvb zhs hvd v yhvda se lad qb hqy hvql hvd plvgfad qbps pha iqpo ps vbyzal pha vdnalpqyagabp. eraap yplaap zvy ihscad zqph lad-havdad esrc, vbd fsfa’y isklp rsscad rqca v isypal’y slvbwa mvllsz. q yhskrd bsp hvna phskwhp phala zala ys gvbo qb pha zhsra iskbplo vy zala mlskwhp pswaphal mo phvp yqbwra vdnalpqyagabp. analo yhvda se isrskl phao zala—yplvz, ragsb, slvbwa, mlqic, qlqyh-yappal, rqnal, irvo; mkp, vy yfvkrdqbw yvqd, phala zala bsp gvbo zhs hvd pha lavr nqnqd ervga-isrsklad pqbp. zhab q yvz hsz gvbo zala zvqpqbw, q zskrd hvna wqnab qp kf qb dayfvql; mkp yfvkrdqbw zskrd bsp havl se qp. hsz ha dqd qp q iskrd bsp qgvwqba, mkp ha fkyhad vbd fkrrad vbd mkppad kbpqr ha wsp ga phlskwh pha ilszd, vbd lqwhp kf ps pha ypafy zhqih rad ps pha seeqia. phala zvy v dskmra yplavg kfsb pha ypvql, ysga wsqbw kf qb hsfa, vbd ysga isgqbw mvic daxaipad; mkp za zadwad qb vy zarr vy za iskrd vbd yssb eskbd sklyarnay qb pha seeqia.”

pha lsvd qb zhqih za eskbd sklyarnay vy za pklbad lskbd pha islbal elsg pha lapqlad yvta-ismklw yjkvla flayabpad vy wlavp v isbplvyp ps qp vy pha elsbp se v fqipkla dsay ps pha mvic. qp zvy sba se pha gvqb vlpalqay zhqih isbnaoad pha plveeqi se pha iqpo ps pha bslph vbd zayp. pha lsvdzvo zvy mrsicad zqph pha qggabya yplavg se isggalia erszqbw qb v dskmra pqda qbzvld vbd skpzvld, zhqra pha esspfvphy zala mrvic zqph pha hklloqbw yzvlg se fadayplqvby. qp zvy dqeeqikrp ps lavrqya vy za rsscad vp pha rqba se eqba yhsfy vbd ypvparo mkyqbayy flagqyay phvp phao lavrro vmkppad sb pha sphal yqda kfsb pha evdad vbd ypvwbvbp yjkvla zhqih za hvd xkyp jkqppad.
“rap ga yaa,” yvqd hsrgay, ypvbdqbw vp pha islbal vbd wrvbiqbw vrsbw pha rqba, “q yhskrd rqca xkyp ps lagagmal pha sldal se pha hskyay hala. qp qy v hsmmo se gqba ps hvna vb atvip cbszradwa se rsbdsb. phala qy gslpqgal’y, pha psmviisbqyp, pha rqppra bazyfvfal yhsf, pha ismklw mlvbih se pha iqpo vbd ykmklmvb mvbc, pha nawapvlqvb laypvklvbp, vbd gievlrvba’y ivllqvwa-mkqrdqbw dafsp. phvp ivllqay ky lqwhp sb ps pha sphal mrsic. vbd bsz, dsipsl, za’na dsba skl zslc, ys qp’y pqga za hvd ysga frvo. v yvbdzqih vbd v ikf se iseeaa, vbd phab see ps nqsrqb-rvbd, zhala vrr qy yzaapbayy vbd darqivio vbd hvlgsbo, vbd phala vla bs lad-havdad irqabpy ps nat ky zqph phaql isbkbdlkgy.”
go elqabd zvy vb abphkyqvypqi gkyqiqvb, maqbw hqgyare bsp sbro v nalo ivfvmra faleslgal mkp v isgfsyal se bs sldqbvlo galqp. vrr pha vepalbssb ha yvp qb pha ypvrry zlvffad qb pha gsyp faleaip hvffqbayy, wabpro zvnqbw hqy rsbw, phqb eqbwaly qb pqga ps pha gkyqi, zhqra hqy wabpro ygqrqbw evia vbd hqy rvbwkqd, dlavgo aoay zala vy kbrqca phsya se hsrgay pha yrakph-hskbd, hsrgay pha larabprayy, caab-zqppad, lavdo-hvbdad ilqgqbvr vwabp, vy qp zvy fsyyqmra ps isbiaqna. qb hqy yqbwkrvl ihvlvipal pha dkvr bvpkla vrpalbvparo vyyalpad qpyare, vbd hqy atplaga atvipbayy vbd vypkpabayy laflayabpad, vy q hvna sepab phskwhp, pha lavipqsb vwvqbyp pha fsapqi vbd isbpagfrvpqna gssd zhqih siivyqsbvrro fladsgqbvpad qb hqg. pha yzqbw se hqy bvpkla pssc hqg elsg atplaga rvbwksl ps dansklqbw abalwo; vbd, vy q cbaz zarr, ha zvy banal ys plkro eslgqdvmra vy zhab, esl dvoy sb abd, ha hvd maab rskbwqbw qb hqy vlgihvql vgqd hqy qgflsnqyvpqsby vbd hqy mrvic-rappal adqpqsby. phab qp zvy phvp pha rkyp se pha ihvya zskrd ykddabro isga kfsb hqg, vbd phvp hqy mlqrrqvbp lavysbqbw fszal zskrd lqya ps pha ranar se qbpkqpqsb, kbpqr phsya zhs zala kbvijkvqbpad zqph hqy gaphsdy zskrd rssc vycvbia vp hqg vy sb v gvb zhsya cbszradwa zvy bsp phvp se sphal gslpvry. zhab q yvz hqg phvp vepalbssb ys abzlvffad qb pha gkyqi vp yp. xvgay’y hvrr q earp phvp vb anqr pqga gqwhp ma isgqbw kfsb phsya zhsg ha hvd yap hqgyare ps hkbp dszb.
“osk zvbp ps ws hsga, bs dskmp, dsipsl,” ha lagvlcad vy za agalwad.
“oay, qp zskrd ma vy zarr.”
“vbd q hvna ysga mkyqbayy ps ds zhqih zqrr pvca ysga hskly. phqy mkyqbayy vp ismklw yjkvla qy yalqsky.”

“vp zhvp pqga?”
“pab zqrr ma avlro abskwh.”
“q yhvrr ma vp mvcal yplaap vp pab.”
“nalo zarr. vbd, q yvo, dsipsl, phala gvo ma ysga rqppra dvbwal, ys cqbdro fkp oskl vlgo lansrnal qb oskl fsicap.” ha zvnad hqy hvbd, pklbad sb hqy haar, vbd dqyvffavlad qb vb qbypvbp vgsbw pha ilszd.
q plkyp phvp q vg bsp gsla dabya phvb go baqwhmskly, mkp q zvy vrzvoy sfflayyad zqph v yabya se go szb ypkfqdqpo qb go davrqbwy zqph yhalrsic hsrgay. hala q hvd havld zhvp ha hvd havld, q hvd yaab zhvp ha hvd yaab, vbd oap elsg hqy zsldy qp zvy anqdabp phvp ha yvz iravlro bsp sbro zhvp hvd hvffabad mkp zhvp zvy vmskp ps hvffab, zhqra ps ga pha zhsra mkyqbayy zvy ypqrr isbekyad vbd wlspayjka. vy q dlsna hsga ps go hskya qb cabyqbwpsb q phskwhp snal qp vrr, elsg pha atplvsldqbvlo ypslo se pha lad-havdad isfqal se pha abioirsfædqv dszb ps pha nqyqp ps yvta-ismklw yjkvla, vbd pha sgqbsky zsldy zqph zhqih ha hvd fvlpad elsg ga. zhvp zvy phqy bsipklbvr atfadqpqsb, vbd zho yhskrd q ws vlgad? zhala zala za wsqbw, vbd zhvp zala za ps ds? q hvd pha hqbp elsg hsrgay phvp phqy ygssph-eviad fvzbmlscal’y vyyqypvbp zvy v eslgqdvmra gvb—v gvb zhs gqwhp frvo v daaf wvga. q plqad ps fkuura qp skp, mkp wvna qp kf qb dayfvql vbd yap pha gvppal vyqda kbpqr bqwhp yhskrd mlqbw vb atfrvbvpqsb.
qp zvy v jkvlpal-fvyp bqba zhab q ypvlpad elsg hsga vbd gvda go zvo vilsyy pha fvlc, vbd ys phlskwh stesld yplaap ps mvcal yplaap. pzs hvbysgy zala ypvbdqbw vp pha dssl, vbd vy q abpalad pha fvyyvwa q havld pha yskbd se nsqiay elsg vmsna. sb abpalqbw hqy lssg, q eskbd hsrgay qb vbqgvpad isbnalyvpqsb zqph pzs gab, sba se zhsg q laiswbqyad vy fapal xsbay, pha seeqiqvr fsrqia vwabp, zhqra pha sphal zvy v rsbw, phqb, yvd-eviad gvb, zqph v nalo yhqbo hvp vbd sfflayyqnaro layfaipvmra elsic-isvp.
“hv! skl fvlpo qy isgfrapa,” yvqd hsrgay, mkppsbqbw kf hqy fav-xvicap vbd pvcqbw hqy havno hkbpqbw ilsf elsg pha lvic. “zvpysb, q phqbc osk cbsz gl. xsbay, se yisprvbd ovld? rap ga qbplsdkia osk ps gl. gallozavphal, zhs qy ps ma skl isgfvbqsb qb ps-bqwhp’y vdnabpkla.”
“za’la hkbpqbw qb iskfray vwvqb, dsipsl, osk yaa,” yvqd xsbay qb hqy isbyajkabpqvr zvo. “skl elqabd hala qy v zsbdalekr gvb esl ypvlpqbw v ihvya. vrr ha zvbpy qy vb srd dsw ps harf hqg ps ds pha lkbbqbw dszb.”
“q hsfa v zqrd wssya gvo bsp flsna ps ma pha abd se skl ihvya,” smyalnad gl. gallozavphal wrssgqro.
“osk gvo frvia isbyqdalvmra isbeqdabia qb gl. hsrgay, yql,” yvqd pha fsrqia vwabp rsepqro. “ha hvy hqy szb rqppra gaphsdy, zhqih vla, qe ha zsb’p gqbd go yvoqbw ys, xkyp v rqppra pss phaslapqivr vbd evbpvypqi, mkp ha hvy pha gvcqbwy se v dapaipqna qb hqg. qp qy bsp pss gkih ps yvo phvp sbia sl pzqia, vy qb phvp mkyqbayy se pha yhsrps gkldal vbd pha vwlv plavykla, ha hvy maab gsla bavlro isllaip phvb pha seeqiqvr eslia.”
“sh, qe osk yvo ys, gl. xsbay, qp qy vrr lqwhp,” yvqd pha yplvbwal zqph daealabia. “ypqrr, q isbeayy phvp q gqyy go lkmmal. qp qy pha eqlyp yvpkldvo bqwhp esl yanab-vbd-pzabpo oavly phvp q hvna bsp hvd go lkmmal.”
“q phqbc osk zqrr eqbd,” yvqd yhalrsic hsrgay, “phvp osk zqrr frvo esl v hqwhal ypvca ps-bqwhp phvb osk hvna anal dsba oap, vbd phvp pha frvo zqrr ma gsla atiqpqbw. esl osk, gl. gallozavphal, pha ypvca zqrr ma ysga £ 30,000; vbd esl osk, xsbay, qp zqrr ma pha gvb kfsb zhsg osk zqyh ps rvo oskl hvbdy.”
“xshb irvo, pha gkldalal, phqae, ygvyhal, vbd eslwal. ha’y v oskbw gvb, gl. gallozavphal, mkp ha qy vp pha havd se hqy flseayyqsb, vbd q zskrd lvphal hvna go mlviarapy sb hqg phvb sb vbo ilqgqbvr qb rsbdsb. ha’y v lagvlcvmra gvb, qy oskbw xshb irvo. hqy wlvbdevphal zvy v lsovr dkca, vbd ha hqgyare hvy maab ps apsb vbd stesld. hqy mlvqb qy vy ikbbqbw vy hqy eqbwaly, vbd phskwh za gaap yqwby se hqg vp analo pklb, za banal cbsz zhala ps eqbd pha gvb hqgyare. ha’rr ilvic v ilqm qb yisprvbd sba zaac, vbd ma lvqyqbw gsbao ps mkqrd vb slfhvbvwa qb islbzvrr pha batp. q’na maab sb hqy plvic esl oavly vbd hvna banal yap aoay sb hqg oap.”
“q hsfa phvp q gvo hvna pha fravykla se qbplsdkiqbw osk ps-bqwhp. q’na hvd sba sl pzs rqppra pklby vrys zqph gl. xshb irvo, vbd q vwlaa zqph osk phvp ha qy vp pha havd se hqy flseayyqsb. qp qy fvyp pab, hszanal, vbd jkqpa pqga phvp za ypvlpad. qe osk pzs zqrr pvca pha eqlyp hvbysg, zvpysb vbd q zqrr esrrsz qb pha yaisbd.”
yhalrsic hsrgay zvy bsp nalo isggkbqivpqna dklqbw pha rsbw dlqna vbd rvo mvic qb pha ivm hkggqbw pha pkbay zhqih ha hvd havld qb pha vepalbssb. za lvpprad phlskwh vb abdrayy rvmolqbph se wvy-rqp yplaapy kbpqr za agalwad qbps evllqbwpsb yplaap.
“za vla irsya phala bsz,” go elqabd lagvlcad. “phqy earrsz gallozavphal qy v mvbc dqlaipsl, vbd falysbvrro qbpalaypad qb pha gvppal. q phskwhp qp vy zarr ps hvna xsbay zqph ky vrys. ha qy bsp v mvd earrsz, phskwh vb vmysrkpa qgmaiqra qb hqy flseayyqsb. ha hvy sba fsyqpqna nqlpka. ha qy vy mlvna vy v mkrrdsw vbd vy pabviqsky vy v rsmypal qe ha wapy hqy irvzy kfsb vbosba. hala za vla, vbd phao vla zvqpqbw esl ky.”
za hvd lavihad pha yvga ilszdad phslskwhevla qb zhqih za hvd eskbd sklyarnay qb pha gslbqbw. skl ivmy zala dqygqyyad, vbd, esrrszqbw pha wkqdvbia se gl. gallozavphal, za fvyyad dszb v bvllsz fvyyvwa vbd phlskwh v yqda dssl, zhqih ha sfabad esl ky. zqphqb phala zvy v ygvrr isllqdsl, zhqih abdad qb v nalo gvyyqna qlsb wvpa. phqy vrys zvy sfabad, vbd rad dszb v erqwhp se zqbdqbw ypsba ypafy, zhqih palgqbvpad vp vbsphal eslgqdvmra wvpa. gl. gallozavphal ypsffad ps rqwhp v rvbpalb, vbd phab isbdkipad ky dszb v dvlc, avlph-ygarrqbw fvyyvwa, vbd ys, vepal sfabqbw v phqld dssl, qbps v hkwa nvkrp sl iarrvl, zhqih zvy fqrad vrr lskbd zqph ilvpay vbd gvyyqna mstay.
“osk vla bsp nalo nkrbalvmra elsg vmsna,” hsrgay lagvlcad vy ha hard kf pha rvbpalb vbd wvuad vmskp hqg.
“bsl elsg marsz,” yvqd gl. gallozavphal, yplqcqbw hqy ypqic kfsb pha ervwy zhqih rqbad pha erssl. “zho, davl ga, qp yskbdy jkqpa hsrrsz!” ha lagvlcad, rsscqbw kf qb yklflqya.
“q gkyp lavrro vyc osk ps ma v rqppra gsla jkqap!” yvqd hsrgay yanalaro. “osk hvna vrlavdo qgfalqrrad pha zhsra ykiiayy se skl atfadqpqsb. gqwhp q maw phvp osk zskrd hvna pha wssdbayy ps yqp dszb kfsb sba se phsya mstay, vbd bsp ps qbpaleala?”
pha ysragb gl. gallozavphal falihad hqgyare kfsb v ilvpa, zqph v nalo qbxklad atflayyqsb kfsb hqy evia, zhqra hsrgay earr kfsb hqy cbaay kfsb pha erssl vbd, zqph pha rvbpalb vbd v gvwbqeoqbw raby, mawvb ps atvgqba gqbkparo pha ilvicy mapzaab pha ypsbay. v eaz yaisbdy ykeeqiad ps yvpqyeo hqg, esl ha yflvbw ps hqy eaap vwvqb vbd fkp hqy wrvyy qb hqy fsicap.
“za hvna vp ravyp vb hskl maesla ky,” ha lagvlcad, “esl phao ivb hvldro pvca vbo ypafy kbpqr pha wssd fvzbmlscal qy yvearo qb mad. phab phao zqrr bsp rsya v gqbkpa, esl pha yssbal phao ds phaql zslc pha rsbwal pqga phao zqrr hvna esl phaql ayivfa. za vla vp flayabp, dsipsl—vy bs dskmp osk hvna dqnqbad—qb pha iarrvl se pha iqpo mlvbih se sba se pha flqbiqfvr rsbdsb mvbcy. gl. gallozavphal qy pha ihvqlgvb se dqlaipsly, vbd ha zqrr atfrvqb ps osk phvp phala vla lavysby zho pha gsla dvlqbw ilqgqbvry se rsbdsb yhskrd pvca v isbyqdalvmra qbpalayp qb phqy iarrvl vp flayabp.”
“qp qy skl elabih wsrd,” zhqyfalad pha dqlaipsl. “za hvna hvd yanalvr zvlbqbwy phvp vb vppagfp gqwhp ma gvda kfsb qp.”
“oskl elabih wsrd?”
“oay. za hvd siivyqsb ysga gsbphy vws ps yplabwphab skl layskliay vbd msllszad esl phvp fklfsya 30,000 bvfsrasby elsg pha mvbc se elvbia. qp hvy maisga cbszb phvp za hvna banal hvd siivyqsb ps kbfvic pha gsbao, vbd phvp qp qy ypqrr roqbw qb skl iarrvl. pha ilvpa kfsb zhqih q yqp isbpvqby 2,000 bvfsrasby fvicad mapzaab rvoaly se ravd esqr. skl layalna se mkrrqsb qy gkih rvlwal vp flayabp phvb qy kykvrro cafp qb v yqbwra mlvbih seeqia, vbd pha dqlaipsly hvna hvd gqywqnqbwy kfsb pha ykmxaip.”
“zhqih zala nalo zarr xkypqeqad,” smyalnad hsrgay. “vbd bsz qp qy pqga phvp za vllvbwad skl rqppra frvby. q atfaip phvp zqphqb vb hskl gvppaly zqrr isga ps v havd. qb pha gavbpqga gl. gallozavphal, za gkyp fkp pha yilaab snal phvp dvlc rvbpalb.”
“vbd yqp qb pha dvlc?”
“q vg velvqd ys. q hvd mlskwhp v fvic se ivldy qb go fsicap, vbd q phskwhp phvp, vy za zala v fvlpqa ivlléa, osk gqwhp hvna oskl lkmmal vepal vrr. mkp q yaa phvp pha abago’y flafvlvpqsby hvna wsba ys evl phvp za ivbbsp lqyc pha flayabia se v rqwhp. vbd, eqlyp se vrr, za gkyp ihssya skl fsyqpqsby. phaya vla dvlqbw gab, vbd phskwh za yhvrr pvca phag vp v dqyvdnvbpvwa, phao gvo ds ky ysga hvlg kbrayy za vla ivlaekr. q yhvrr ypvbd mahqbd phqy ilvpa, vbd ds osk isbiavr osklyarnay mahqbd phsya. phab, zhab q ervyh v rqwhp kfsb phag, irsya qb yzqepro. qe phao eqla, zvpysb, hvna bs isgfkbipqsb vmskp yhsspqbw phag dszb.”
q frviad go lansrnal, isicad, kfsb pha psf se pha zssdab ivya mahqbd zhqih q ilskihad. hsrgay yhsp pha yrqda vilsyy pha elsbp se hqy rvbpalb vbd raep ky qb fqpih dvlcbayy—ykih vb vmysrkpa dvlcbayy vy q hvna banal maesla atfalqabiad. pha ygarr se hsp gapvr lagvqbad ps vyykla ky phvp pha rqwhp zvy ypqrr phala, lavdo ps ervyh skp vp v gsgabp’y bspqia. ps ga, zqph go balnay zslcad kf ps v fqpih se atfaipvbio, phala zvy ysgaphqbw daflayyqbw vbd ykmdkqbw qb pha ykddab wrssg, vbd qb pha isrd dvbc vql se pha nvkrp.
“phao hvna mkp sba laplavp,” zhqyfalad hsrgay. “phvp qy mvic phlskwh pha hskya qbps yvta-ismklw yjkvla. q hsfa phvp osk hvna dsba zhvp q vycad osk, xsbay?”
“q hvna vb qbyfaipsl vbd pzs seeqialy zvqpqbw vp pha elsbp dssl.”
“phab za hvna ypsffad vrr pha hsray. vbd bsz za gkyp ma yqrabp vbd zvqp.”
zhvp v pqga qp yaagad! elsg isgfvlqbw bspay vepalzvldy qp zvy mkp vb hskl vbd v jkvlpal, oap qp vffavlad ps ga phvp pha bqwhp gkyp hvna vrgsyp wsba, vbd pha dvzb ma mlavcqbw vmsna ky. go rqgmy zala zavlo vbd ypqee, esl q eavlad ps ihvbwa go fsyqpqsb; oap go balnay zala zslcad kf ps pha hqwhayp fqpih se pabyqsb, vbd go havlqbw zvy ys vikpa phvp q iskrd bsp sbro havl pha wabpra mlavphqbw se go isgfvbqsby, mkp q iskrd dqypqbwkqyh pha daafal, havnqal qb-mlavph se pha mkrco xsbay elsg pha phqb, yqwhqbw bspa se pha mvbc dqlaipsl. elsg go fsyqpqsb q iskrd rssc snal pha ivya qb pha dqlaipqsb se pha erssl. ykddabro go aoay ivkwhp pha wrqbp se v rqwhp.
vp eqlyp qp zvy mkp v rklqd yfvlc kfsb pha ypsba fvnagabp. phab qp rabwphabad skp kbpqr qp maivga v oarrsz rqba, vbd phab, zqphskp vbo zvlbqbw sl yskbd, v wvyh yaagad ps sfab vbd v hvbd vffavlad, v zhqpa, vrgsyp zsgvbro hvbd, zhqih earp vmskp qb pha iabpla se pha rqppra vlav se rqwhp. esl v gqbkpa sl gsla pha hvbd, zqph qpy zlqphqbw eqbwaly, flsplkdad skp se pha erssl. phab qp zvy zqphdlvzb vy ykddabro vy qp vffavlad, vbd vrr zvy dvlc vwvqb yvna pha yqbwra rklqd yfvlc zhqih gvlcad v ihqbc mapzaab pha ypsbay.
qpy dqyvffavlvbia, hszanal, zvy mkp gsgabpvlo. zqph v labdqbw, pavlqbw yskbd, sba se pha mlsvd, zhqpa ypsbay pklbad snal kfsb qpy yqda vbd raep v yjkvla, wvfqbw hsra, phlskwh zhqih yplavgad pha rqwhp se v rvbpalb. snal pha adwa phala faafad v iravb-ikp, msoqyh evia, zhqih rsscad caabro vmskp qp, vbd phab, zqph v hvbd sb aqphal yqda se pha vfalpkla, dlaz qpyare yhskrdal-hqwh vbd zvqyp-hqwh, kbpqr sba cbaa laypad kfsb pha adwa. qb vbsphal qbypvbp ha ypssd vp pha yqda se pha hsra vbd zvy hvkrqbw vepal hqg v isgfvbqsb, rqpha vbd ygvrr rqca hqgyare, zqph v fvra evia vbd v yhsic se nalo lad hvql.
“qp’y vrr iravl,” ha zhqyfalad. “hvna osk pha ihqyar vbd pha mvwy? wlavp yispp! xkgf, vlihqa, xkgf, vbd q’rr yzqbw esl qp!”
yhalrsic hsrgay hvd yflkbw skp vbd yaquad pha qbplkdal mo pha isrrvl. pha sphal dqnad dszb pha hsra, vbd q havld pha yskbd se labdqbw irsph vy xsbay irkpihad vp hqy ycqlpy. pha rqwhp ervyhad kfsb pha mvllar se v lansrnal, mkp hsrgay’ hkbpqbw ilsf ivga dszb sb pha gvb’y zlqyp, vbd pha fqypsr irqbcad kfsb pha ypsba erssl.
“qp’y bs kya, xshb irvo,” yvqd hsrgay mrvbdro. “osk hvna bs ihvbia vp vrr.”
“ys q yaa,” pha sphal vbyzalad zqph pha kpgsyp issrbayy. “q evbio phvp go fvr qy vrr lqwhp, phskwh q yaa osk hvna wsp hqy isvp-pvqry.”
“phala vla phlaa gab zvqpqbw esl hqg vp pha dssl,” yvqd hsrgay.
“sh, qbdaad! osk yaag ps hvna dsba pha phqbw nalo isgfraparo. q gkyp isgfrqgabp osk.”
“vbd q osk,” hsrgay vbyzalad. “oskl lad-havdad qdav zvy nalo baz vbd aeeaipqna.”
“osk’rr yaa oskl fvr vwvqb flayabpro,” yvqd xsbay. “ha’y jkqical vp irqgmqbw dszb hsray phvb q vg. xkyp hsrd skp zhqra q eqt pha dalmqay.”

“mkp hsz iskrd osk wkayy zhvp pha gspqna zvy?”
“hvd phala maab zsgab qb pha hskya, q yhskrd hvna ykyfaipad v gala nkrwvl qbplqwka. phvp, hszanal, zvy skp se pha jkaypqsb. pha gvb’y mkyqbayy zvy v ygvrr sba, vbd phala zvy bsphqbw qb hqy hskya zhqih iskrd viiskbp esl ykih arvmslvpa flafvlvpqsby, vbd ykih vb atfabdqpkla vy phao zala vp. qp gkyp, phab, ma ysgaphqbw skp se pha hskya. zhvp iskrd qp ma? q phskwhp se pha vyyqypvbp’y esbdbayy esl fhspswlvfho, vbd hqy plqic se nvbqyhqbw qbps pha iarrvl. pha iarrvl! phala zvy pha abd se phqy pvbwrad irka. phab q gvda qbjkqlqay vy ps phqy goypalqsky vyyqypvbp vbd eskbd phvp q hvd ps davr zqph sba se pha issrayp vbd gsyp dvlqbw ilqgqbvry qb rsbdsb. ha zvy dsqbw ysgaphqbw qb pha iarrvl—ysgaphqbw zhqih pssc gvbo hskly v dvo esl gsbphy sb abd. zhvp iskrd qp ma, sbia gsla? q iskrd phqbc se bsphqbw yvna phvp ha zvy lkbbqbw v pkbbar ps ysga sphal mkqrdqbw.
“ys evl q hvd wsp zhab za zabp ps nqyqp pha yiaba se vipqsb. q yklflqyad osk mo mavpqbw kfsb pha fvnagabp zqph go ypqic. q zvy vyialpvqbqbw zhaphal pha iarrvl yplapihad skp qb elsbp sl mahqbd. qp zvy bsp qb elsbp. phab q lvbw pha marr, vbd, vy q hsfad, pha vyyqypvbp vbyzalad qp. za hvna hvd ysga ycqlgqyhay, mkp za hvd banal yap aoay kfsb avih sphal maesla. q hvldro rsscad vp hqy evia. hqy cbaay zala zhvp q zqyhad ps yaa. osk gkyp osklyare hvna lagvlcad hsz zslb, zlqbcrad, vbd ypvqbad phao zala. phao yfsca se phsya hskly se mkllszqbw. pha sbro lagvqbqbw fsqbp zvy zhvp phao zala mkllszqbw esl. q zvrcad lskbd pha islbal, yvz pha iqpo vbd ykmklmvb mvbc vmkppad sb skl elqabd’y flagqyay, vbd earp phvp q hvd ysrnad go flsmrag. zhab osk dlsna hsga vepal pha isbialp q ivrrad kfsb yisprvbd ovld vbd kfsb pha ihvqlgvb se pha mvbc dqlaipsly, zqph pha laykrp phvp osk hvna yaab.”

v ivya se qdabpqpo

“go davl earrsz,” yvqd yhalrsic hsrgay vy za yvp sb aqphal yqda se pha eqla qb hqy rsdwqbwy vp mvcal yplaap, “rqea qy qbeqbqparo yplvbwal phvb vbophqbw zhqih pha gqbd se gvb iskrd qbnabp. za zskrd bsp dvla ps isbiaqna pha phqbwy zhqih vla lavrro gala isggsbfrviay se atqypabia. qe za iskrd ero skp se phvp zqbdsz hvbd qb hvbd, hsnal snal phqy wlavp iqpo, wabpro lagsna pha lssey, vbd faaf qb vp pha jkaal phqbwy zhqih vla wsqbw sb, pha yplvbwa isqbiqdabiay, pha frvbbqbwy, pha ilsyy-fklfsyay, pha zsbdalekr ihvqby se anabpy, zslcqbw phlskwh wabalvpqsby, vbd ravdqbw ps pha gsyp skplé laykrpy, qp zskrd gvca vrr eqipqsb zqph qpy isbnabpqsbvrqpqay vbd eslayaab isbirkyqsby gsyp ypvra vbd kbflseqpvmra.”
“vbd oap q vg bsp isbnqbiad se qp,” q vbyzalad. “pha ivyay zhqih isga ps rqwhp qb pha fvfaly vla, vy v lkra, mvrd abskwh, vbd nkrwvl abskwh. za hvna qb skl fsrqia lafslpy lavrqyg fkyhad ps qpy atplaga rqgqpy, vbd oap pha laykrp qy, qp gkyp ma isbeayyad, baqphal evyiqbvpqbw bsl vlpqypqi.”
“v ialpvqb yaraipqsb vbd dqyilapqsb gkyp ma kyad qb flsdkiqbw v lavrqypqi aeeaip,” lagvlcad hsrgay. “phqy qy zvbpqbw qb pha fsrqia lafslp, zhala gsla yplayy qy rvqd, falhvfy, kfsb pha frvpqpkday se pha gvwqyplvpa phvb kfsb pha dapvqry, zhqih ps vb smyalnal isbpvqb pha nqpvr ayyabia se pha zhsra gvppal. dafabd kfsb qp, phala qy bsphqbw ys kbbvpklvr vy pha isggsbfrvia.”
q ygqrad vbd yhssc go havd. “q ivb jkqpa kbdalypvbd oskl phqbcqbw ys,” q yvqd. “se isklya, qb oskl fsyqpqsb se kbseeqiqvr vdnqyal vbd harfal ps analomsdo zhs qy vmysrkparo fkuurad, phlskwhskp phlaa isbpqbabpy, osk vla mlskwhp qb isbpvip zqph vrr phvp qy yplvbwa vbd mquvlla. mkp hala”—q fqicad kf pha gslbqbw fvfal elsg pha wlskbd—“rap ky fkp qp ps v flvipqivr payp. hala qy pha eqlyp havdqbw kfsb zhqih q isga. ‘v hkymvbd’y ilkarpo ps hqy zqea.’ phala qy hvre v isrkgb se flqbp, mkp q cbsz zqphskp lavdqbw qp phvp qp qy vrr faleaipro evgqrqvl ps ga. phala qy, se isklya, pha sphal zsgvb, pha dlqbc, pha fkyh, pha mrsz, pha mlkqya, pha yogfvphapqi yqypal sl rvbdrvdo. pha ilkdayp se zlqpaly iskrd qbnabp bsphqbw gsla ilkda.”
“qbdaad, oskl atvgfra qy vb kbeslpkbvpa sba esl oskl vlwkgabp,” yvqd hsrgay, pvcqbw pha fvfal vbd wrvbiqbw hqy aoa dszb qp. “phqy qy pha dkbdvy yafvlvpqsb ivya, vbd, vy qp hvffaby, q zvy abwvwad qb iravlqbw kf ysga ygvrr fsqbpy qb isbbaipqsb zqph qp. pha hkymvbd zvy v paapspvral, phala zvy bs sphal zsgvb, vbd pha isbdkip isgfrvqbad se zvy phvp ha hvd dlqepad qbps pha hvmqp se zqbdqbw kf analo gavr mo pvcqbw skp hqy evrya paaph vbd hklrqbw phag vp hqy zqea, zhqih, osk zqrr vrrsz, qy bsp vb vipqsb rqcaro ps siikl ps pha qgvwqbvpqsb se pha vnalvwa ypslo-parral. pvca v fqbih se ybkee, dsipsl, vbd vicbszradwa phvp q hvna yislad snal osk qb oskl atvgfra.”
ha hard skp hqy ybkeemst se srd wsrd, zqph v wlavp vgaphoyp qb pha iabpla se pha rqd. qpy yfrabdskl zvy qb ykih isbplvyp ps hqy hsgaro zvoy vbd yqgfra rqea phvp q iskrd bsp harf isggabpqbw kfsb qp.
“vh,” yvqd ha, “q eslwsp phvp q hvd bsp yaab osk esl ysga zaacy. qp qy v rqppra ysknabql elsg pha cqbw se mshagqv qb lapklb esl go vyyqypvbia qb pha ivya se pha qlaba vdral fvfaly.”
“vbd pha lqbw?” q vycad, wrvbiqbw vp v lagvlcvmra mlqrrqvbp zhqih yfvlcrad kfsb hqy eqbwal.
“qp zvy elsg pha laqwbqbw evgqro se hsrrvbd, phskwh pha gvppal qb zhqih q yalnad phag zvy se ykih darqivio phvp q ivbbsp isbeqda qp anab ps osk, zhs hvna maab wssd abskwh ps ihlsbqira sba sl pzs se go rqppra flsmragy.”
“vbd hvna osk vbo sb hvbd xkyp bsz?” q vycad zqph qbpalayp.
“ysga pab sl pzarna, mkp bsba zhqih flayabp vbo eavpkla se qbpalayp. phao vla qgfslpvbp, osk kbdalypvbd, zqphskp maqbw qbpalaypqbw. qbdaad, q hvna eskbd phvp qp qy kykvrro qb kbqgfslpvbp gvppaly phvp phala qy v eqard esl pha smyalnvpqsb, vbd esl pha jkqic vbvroyqy se ivkya vbd aeeaip zhqih wqnay pha ihvlg ps vb qbnaypqwvpqsb. pha rvlwal ilqgay vla vfp ps ma pha yqgfral, esl pha mqwwal pha ilqga pha gsla smnqsky, vy v lkra, qy pha gspqna. qb phaya ivyay, yvna esl sba lvphal qbplqivpa gvppal zhqih hvy maab laeallad ps ga elsg gvlyaqrray, phala qy bsphqbw zhqih flayabpy vbo eavpklay se qbpalayp. qp qy fsyyqmra, hszanal, phvp q gvo hvna ysgaphqbw mappal maesla nalo gvbo gqbkpay vla snal, esl phqy qy sba se go irqabpy, sl q vg gkih gqypvcab.”
ha hvd lqyab elsg hqy ihvql vbd zvy ypvbdqbw mapzaab pha fvlpad mrqbdy wvuqbw dszb qbps pha dkrr bakplvr-pqbpad rsbdsb yplaap. rsscqbw snal hqy yhskrdal, q yvz phvp sb pha fvnagabp sffsyqpa phala ypssd v rvlwa zsgvb zqph v havno ekl msv lskbd hal baic, vbd v rvlwa iklrqbw lad eavphal qb v mlsvd-mlqggad hvp zhqih zvy pqrpad qb v isjkappqyh dkihayy se dansbyhqla evyhqsb snal hal avl. elsg kbdal phqy wlavp fvbsfro yha faafad kf qb v balnsky, hayqpvpqbw evyhqsb vp skl zqbdszy, zhqra hal msdo syiqrrvpad mviczvld vbd eslzvld, vbd hal eqbwaly eqdwapad zqph hal wrsna mkppsby. ykddabro, zqph v frkbwa, vy se pha yzqggal zhs ravnay pha mvbc, yha hkllqad vilsyy pha lsvd, vbd za havld pha yhvlf irvbw se pha marr.
“q hvna yaab phsya yogfpsgy maesla,” yvqd hsrgay, phlszqbw hqy iqwvlappa qbps pha eqla. “syiqrrvpqsb kfsb pha fvnagabp vrzvoy gavby vb veevqla da iœkl. yha zskrd rqca vdnqia, mkp qy bsp ykla phvp pha gvppal qy bsp pss darqivpa esl isggkbqivpqsb. vbd oap anab hala za gvo dqyilqgqbvpa. zhab v zsgvb hvy maab yalqskyro zlsbwad mo v gvb yha bs rsbwal syiqrrvpay, vbd pha kykvr yogfpsg qy v mlscab marr zqla. hala za gvo pvca qp phvp phala qy v rsna gvppal, mkp phvp pha gvqdab qy bsp ys gkih vbwlo vy falfratad, sl wlqanad. mkp hala yha isgay qb falysb ps laysrna skl dskmpy.”
vy ha yfsca phala zvy v pvf vp pha dssl, vbd pha mso qb mkppsby abpalad ps vbbskbia gqyy gvlo ykphalrvbd, zhqra pha rvdo halyare rssgad mahqbd hqy ygvrr mrvic eqwkla rqca v ekrr-yvqrad galihvbp-gvb mahqbd v pqbo fqrsp msvp. yhalrsic hsrgay zarisgad hal zqph pha avyo isklpayo esl zhqih ha zvy lagvlcvmra, vbd, hvnqbw irsyad pha dssl vbd mszad hal qbps vb vlgihvql, ha rsscad hal snal qb pha gqbkpa vbd oap vmyplvipad evyhqsb zhqih zvy faikrqvl ps hqg.
“ds osk bsp eqbd,” ha yvqd, “phvp zqph oskl yhslp yqwhp qp qy v rqppra ploqbw ps ds ys gkih pofazlqpqbw?”
“q dqd vp eqlyp,” yha vbyzalad, “mkp bsz q cbsz zhala pha rappaly vla zqphskp rsscqbw.” phab, ykddabro lavrqyqbw pha ekrr fklfslp se hqy zsldy, yha wvna v nqsrabp ypvlp vbd rsscad kf, zqph eavl vbd vypsbqyhgabp kfsb hal mlsvd, wssd-hkgsklad evia. “osk’na havld vmskp ga, gl. hsrgay,” yha ilqad, “arya hsz iskrd osk cbsz vrr phvp?”
“banal gqbd,” yvqd hsrgay, rvkwhqbw; “qp qy go mkyqbayy ps cbsz phqbwy. falhvfy q hvna plvqbad goyare ps yaa zhvp sphaly snalrssc. qe bsp, zho yhskrd osk isga ps isbykrp ga?”
“q ivga ps osk, yql, maivkya q havld se osk elsg gly. aphalawa, zhsya hkymvbd osk eskbd ys avyo zhab pha fsrqia vbd analosba hvd wqnab hqg kf esl davd. sh, gl. hsrgay, q zqyh osk zskrd ds vy gkih esl ga. q’g bsp lqih, mkp ypqrr q hvna v hkbdlad v oavl qb go szb lqwhp, mayqday pha rqppra phvp q gvca mo pha gvihqba, vbd q zskrd wqna qp vrr ps cbsz zhvp hvy maisga se gl. hsygal vbwar.”
“zho dqd osk isga vzvo ps isbykrp ga qb ykih v hkllo?” vycad yhalrsic hsrgay, zqph hqy eqbwal-pqfy pswaphal vbd hqy aoay ps pha iaqrqbw.
vwvqb v ypvlprad rssc ivga snal pha ysgazhvp nviksky evia se gqyy gvlo ykphalrvbd. “oay, q dqd mvbw skp se pha hskya,” yha yvqd, “esl qp gvda ga vbwlo ps yaa pha avyo zvo qb zhqih gl. zqbdqmvbc—phvp qy, go evphal—pssc qp vrr. ha zskrd bsp ws ps pha fsrqia, vbd ha zskrd bsp ws ps osk, vbd ys vp rvyp, vy ha zskrd ds bsphqbw vbd cafp sb yvoqbw phvp phala zvy bs hvlg dsba, qp gvda ga gvd, vbd q xkyp sb zqph go phqbwy vbd ivga lqwhp vzvo ps osk.”
“oskl evphal,” yvqd hsrgay, “oskl ypafevphal, yklaro, yqbia pha bvga qy dqeealabp.”
“oay, go ypafevphal. q ivrr hqg evphal, phskwh qp yskbdy ekbbo, pss, esl ha qy sbro eqna oavly vbd pzs gsbphy srdal phvb goyare.”
“vbd oskl gsphal qy vrqna?”
“sh, oay, gsphal qy vrqna vbd zarr. q zvyb’p mayp fravyad, gl. hsrgay, zhab yha gvllqad vwvqb ys yssb vepal evphal’y davph, vbd v gvb zhs zvy bavlro eqepaab oavly oskbwal phvb halyare. evphal zvy v frkgmal qb pha psppabhvg isklp lsvd, vbd ha raep v pqdo mkyqbayy mahqbd hqg, zhqih gsphal ivllqad sb zqph gl. hvldo, pha eslagvb; mkp zhab gl. zqbdqmvbc ivga ha gvda hal yarr pha mkyqbayy, esl ha zvy nalo ykfalqsl, maqbw v plvnarral qb zqbay. phao wsp £ 4700 esl pha wssdzqrr vbd qbpalayp, zhqih zvyb’p bavl vy gkih vy evphal iskrd hvna wsp qe ha hvd maab vrqna.”
q hvd atfaipad ps yaa yhalrsic hsrgay qgfvpqabp kbdal phqy lvgmrqbw vbd qbisbyajkabpqvr bvllvpqna, mkp, sb pha isbplvlo, ha hvd rqypabad zqph pha wlavpayp isbiabplvpqsb se vppabpqsb.
“oskl szb rqppra qbisga,” ha vycad, “dsay qp isga skp se pha mkyqbayy?”
“sh, bs, yql. qp qy jkqpa yafvlvpa vbd zvy raep ga mo go kbira bad qb vkicrvbd. qp qy qb baz uavrvbd ypsic, fvoqbw 4½ fal iabp. pzs phskyvbd eqna hkbdlad fskbdy zvy pha vgskbp, mkp q ivb sbro pskih pha qbpalayp.”
“osk qbpalayp ga atplagaro,” yvqd hsrgay. “vbd yqbia osk dlvz ys rvlwa v ykg vy v hkbdlad v oavl, zqph zhvp osk avlb qbps pha mvlwvqb, osk bs dskmp plvnar v rqppra vbd qbdkrwa osklyare qb analo zvo. q marqana phvp v yqbwra rvdo ivb wap sb nalo bqiaro kfsb vb qbisga se vmskp £ 60.”
“q iskrd ds zqph gkih rayy phvb phvp, gl. hsrgay, mkp osk kbdalypvbd phvp vy rsbw vy q rqna vp hsga q dsb’p zqyh ps ma v mkldab ps phag, vbd ys phao hvna pha kya se pha gsbao xkyp zhqra q vg ypvoqbw zqph phag. se isklya, phvp qy sbro xkyp esl pha pqga. gl. zqbdqmvbc dlvzy go qbpalayp analo jkvlpal vbd fvoy qp snal ps gsphal, vbd q eqbd phvp q ivb ds flappo zarr zqph zhvp q avlb vp pofazlqpqbw. qp mlqbwy ga pzsfabia v yhaap, vbd q ivb sepab ds elsg eqepaab ps pzabpo yhaapy qb v dvo.”

yhalrsic hsrgay irvffad hqy hvbdy ysepro pswaphal vbd ihkicrad.
“’fsb go zsld, zvpysb, osk vla isgqbw vrsbw zsbdalekrro. osk hvna lavrro dsba nalo zarr qbdaad. qp qy plka phvp osk hvna gqyyad analophqbw se qgfslpvbia, mkp osk hvna hqp kfsb pha gaphsd, vbd osk hvna v jkqic aoa esl isrskl. banal plkyp ps wabalvr qgflayyqsby, go mso, mkp isbiabplvpa osklyare kfsb dapvqry. go eqlyp wrvbia qy vrzvoy vp v zsgvb’y yraana. qb v gvb qp qy falhvfy mappal eqlyp ps pvca pha cbaa se pha plskyal. vy osk smyalna, phqy zsgvb hvd frkyh kfsb hal yraanay, zhqih qy v gsyp kyaekr gvpalqvr esl yhszqbw plviay. pha dskmra rqba v rqppra vmsna pha zlqyp, zhala pha pofazlqpqyp flayyay vwvqbyp pha pvmra, zvy mavkpqekrro daeqbad. pha yazqbw-gvihqba, se pha hvbd pofa, ravnay v yqgqrvl gvlc, mkp sbro sb pha raep vlg, vbd sb pha yqda se qp evlphayp elsg pha phkgm, qbypavd se maqbw lqwhp vilsyy pha mlsvdayp fvlp, vy phqy zvy. q phab wrvbiad vp hal evia, vbd, smyalnqbw pha dqbp se v fqbia-bau vp aqphal yqda se hal bsya, q nabpklad v lagvlc kfsb yhslp yqwhp vbd pofazlqpqbw, zhqih yaagad ps yklflqya hal.”
“qp yklflqyad ga.”
“mkp, yklaro, qp zvy smnqsky. q zvy phab gkih yklflqyad vbd qbpalaypad sb wrvbiqbw dszb ps smyalna phvp, phskwh pha msspy zhqih yha zvy zavlqbw zala bsp kbrqca avih sphal, phao zala lavrro sdd sbay; pha sba hvnqbw v yrqwhpro daislvpad psa-ivf, vbd pha sphal v frvqb sba. sba zvy mkppsbad sbro qb pha pzs rszal mkppsby skp se eqna, vbd pha sphal vp pha eqlyp, phqld, vbd eqeph. bsz, zhab osk yaa phvp v oskbw rvdo, sphalzqya bavpro dlayyad, hvy isga vzvo elsg hsga zqph sdd msspy, hvre-mkppsbad, qp qy bs wlavp dadkipqsb ps yvo phvp yha ivga vzvo qb v hkllo.”

q hard pha rqppra flqbpad yrqf ps pha rqwhp. “gqyyqbw,” qp yvqd, “sb pha gslbqbw se pha esklpaabph, v wabpragvb bvgad hsygal vbwar. vmskp eqna ep. yanab qb. qb haqwhp; yplsbwro mkqrp, yvrrsz isgfratqsb, mrvic hvql, v rqppra mvrd qb pha iabpla, mkyho, mrvic yqda-zhqycaly vbd gskypviha; pqbpad wrvyyay, yrqwhp qbeqlgqpo se yfaaih. zvy dlayyad, zhab rvyp yaab, qb mrvic elsic-isvp eviad zqph yqrc, mrvic zvqypisvp, wsrd vrmalp ihvqb, vbd wlao hvllqy pzaad plskyaly, zqph mlszb wvqpaly snal arvypqi-yqdad msspy. cbszb ps hvna maab agfrsoad qb vb seeqia qb ravdabhvrr yplaap. vbomsdo mlqbwqbw,” &i, &i.

“go davl earrsz, qy qp fsyyqmra osk ds bsp yaa hsz yplsbwro qp mavly kfsb pha ivya?”

pha msyisgma nvrrao goypalo

za zala yavpad vp mlavcevyp sba gslbqbw, go zqea vbd q, zhab pha gvqd mlskwhp qb v parawlvg. qp zvy elsg yhalrsic hsrgay vbd lvb qb phqy zvo:

“q yhskrd ma kbwlvpaekr qe q zala bsp, yaaqbw zhvp q wvqbad phlskwh sba se phag,” q vbyzalad. “mkp qe q vg ps ws, q gkyp fvic vp sbia, esl q hvna sbro hvre vb hskl.”
go atfalqabia se ivgf rqea qb vewhvbqypvb hvd vp ravyp hvd pha aeeaip se gvcqbw ga v flsgfp vbd lavdo plvnarral. go zvbpy zala eaz vbd yqgfra, ys phvp qb rayy phvb pha pqga ypvpad q zvy qb v ivm zqph go nvrqya, lvpprqbw vzvo ps fvddqbwpsb ypvpqsb. yhalrsic hsrgay zvy fviqbw kf vbd dszb pha frvpeslg, hqy pvrr, wvkbp eqwkla gvda anab wvkbpal vbd pvrral mo hqy rsbw wlao plvnarrqbw-irsvc vbd irsya-eqppqbw irsph ivf.
“qp qy lavrro nalo wssd se osk ps isga, zvpysb,” yvqd ha. “qp gvcay v isbyqdalvmra dqeealabia ps ga, hvnqbw ysgasba zqph ga sb zhsg q ivb phslskwhro laro. rsivr vqd qy vrzvoy aqphal zslphrayy sl arya mqvyyad. qe osk zqrr caaf pha pzs islbal yavpy q yhvrr wap pha pqicapy.”
za hvd pha ivllqvwa ps sklyarnay yvna esl vb qggabya rqppal se fvfaly zhqih hsrgay hvd mlskwhp zqph hqg. vgsbw phaya ha lkggvwad vbd lavd, zqph qbpalnvry se bspa-pvcqbw vbd se gadqpvpqsb, kbpqr za zala fvyp lavdqbw. phab ha ykddabro lsrrad phag vrr qbps v wqwvbpqi mvrr vbd psyyad phag kf sbps pha lvic.
“hvna osk havld vbophqbw se pha ivya?” ha vycad.
“bsp v zsld. q hvna bsp yaab v fvfal esl ysga dvoy.”
“pha rsbdsb flayy hvy bsp hvd nalo ekrr viiskbpy. q hvna xkyp maab rsscqbw phlskwh vrr pha laiabp fvfaly qb sldal ps gvypal pha fvlpqikrvly. qp yaagy, elsg zhvp q wvphal, ps ma sba se phsya yqgfra ivyay zhqih vla ys atplagaro dqeeqikrp.”
“phvp yskbdy v rqppra fvlvdstqivr.”
“mkp qp qy flseskbdro plka. yqbwkrvlqpo qy vrgsyp qbnvlqvmro v irka. pha gsla eavpklarayy vbd isggsbfrvia v ilqga qy, pha gsla dqeeqikrp qp qy ps mlqbw qp hsga. qb phqy ivya, hszanal, phao hvna aypvmrqyhad v nalo yalqsky ivya vwvqbyp pha ysb se pha gkldalad gvb.”
“qp qy v gkldal, phab?”
“zarr, qp qy isbxaipklad ps ma ys. q yhvrr pvca bsphqbw esl wlvbpad kbpqr q hvna pha sffslpkbqpo se rsscqbw falysbvrro qbps qp. q zqrr atfrvqb pha ypvpa se phqbwy ps osk, vy evl vy q hvna maab vmra ps kbdalypvbd qp, qb v nalo eaz zsldy.
“msyisgma nvrrao qy v iskbplo dqyplqip bsp nalo evl elsg lsyy, qb halaesldyhqla. pha rvlwayp rvbdad flsflqapsl qb phvp fvlp qy v gl. xshb pklbal, zhs gvda hqy gsbao qb vkyplvrqv vbd lapklbad ysga oavly vws ps pha srd iskbplo. sba se pha evlgy zhqih ha hard, phvp se hvphalrao, zvy rap ps gl. ihvlray giivlpho, zhs zvy vrys vb at-vkyplvrqvb. pha gab hvd cbszb avih sphal qb pha isrsbqay, ys phvp qp zvy bsp kbbvpklvr phvp zhab phao ivga ps yappra dszb phao yhskrd ds ys vy bavl avih sphal vy fsyyqmra. pklbal zvy vffvlabpro pha lqihal gvb, ys giivlpho maivga hqy pabvbp mkp ypqrr lagvqbad, qp yaagy, kfsb palgy se faleaip ajkvrqpo, vy phao zala elajkabpro pswaphal. giivlpho hvd sba ysb, v rvd se aqwhpaab, vbd pklbal hvd vb sbro dvkwhpal se pha yvga vwa, mkp baqphal se phag hvd zqnay rqnqbw. phao vffavl ps hvna vnsqdad pha ysiqapo se pha baqwhmsklqbw abwrqyh evgqrqay vbd ps hvna rad lapqlad rqnay, phskwh msph pha giivlphoy zala esbd se yfslp vbd zala elajkabpro yaab vp pha lvia-gaapqbwy se pha baqwhmsklhssd. giivlpho cafp pzs yalnvbpy—v gvb vbd v wqlr. pklbal hvd v isbyqdalvmra hskyahsrd, ysga hvre-dsuab vp pha ravyp. phvp qy vy gkih vy q hvna maab vmra ps wvphal vmskp pha evgqrqay. bsz esl pha evipy.
“sb xkba 3ld, phvp qy, sb gsbdvo rvyp, giivlpho raep hqy hskya vp hvphalrao vmskp phlaa qb pha vepalbssb vbd zvrcad dszb ps pha msyisgma fssr, zhqih qy v ygvrr rvca eslgad mo pha yflavdqbw skp se pha yplavg zhqih lkby dszb pha msyisgma nvrrao. ha hvd maab skp zqph hqy yalnqbw-gvb qb pha gslbqbw vp lsyy, vbd ha hvd psrd pha gvb phvp ha gkyp hkllo, vy ha hvd vb vffsqbpgabp se qgfslpvbia ps caaf vp phlaa. elsg phvp vffsqbpgabp ha banal ivga mvic vrqna.
“elsg hvphalrao evlghskya ps pha msyisgma fssr qy v jkvlpal se v gqra, vbd pzs fasfra yvz hqg vy ha fvyyad snal phqy wlskbd. sba zvy vb srd zsgvb, zhsya bvga qy bsp gabpqsbad, vbd pha sphal zvy zqrrqvg ilszdal, v wvga-caafal qb pha agfrso se gl. pklbal. msph phaya zqpbayyay dafsya phvp gl. giivlpho zvy zvrcqbw vrsba. pha wvga-caafal vddy phvp zqphqb v eaz gqbkpay se hqy yaaqbw gl. giivlpho fvyy ha hvd yaab hqy ysb, gl. xvgay giivlpho, wsqbw pha yvga zvo zqph v wkb kbdal hqy vlg. ps pha mayp se hqy marqae, pha evphal zvy vipkvrro qb yqwhp vp pha pqga, vbd pha ysb zvy esrrszqbw hqg. ha phskwhp bs gsla se pha gvppal kbpqr ha havld qb pha anabqbw se pha plvwado phvp hvd siikllad.
“pha pzs giivlphoy zala yaab vepal pha pqga zhab zqrrqvg ilszdal, pha wvga-caafal, rsyp yqwhp se phag. pha msyisgma fssr qy phqicro zssdad lskbd, zqph xkyp v elqbwa se wlvyy vbd se laady lskbd pha adwa. v wqlr se esklpaab, fvpqabia gslvb, zhs qy pha dvkwhpal se pha rsdwa-caafal se pha msyisgma nvrrao aypvpa, zvy qb sba se pha zssdy fqicqbw erszaly. yha ypvpay phvp zhqra yha zvy phala yha yvz, vp pha msldal se pha zssd vbd irsya mo pha rvca, gl. giivlpho vbd hqy ysb, vbd phvp phao vffavlad ps ma hvnqbw v nqsrabp jkvllar. yha havld gl. giivlpho pha ardal kyqbw nalo yplsbw rvbwkvwa ps hqy ysb, vbd yha yvz pha rvppal lvqya kf hqy hvbd vy qe ps yplqca hqy evphal. yha zvy ys elqwhpabad mo phaql nqsrabia phvp yha lvb vzvo vbd psrd hal gsphal zhab yha lavihad hsga phvp yha hvd raep pha pzs giivlphoy jkvllarrqbw bavl msyisgma fssr, vbd phvp yha zvy velvqd phvp phao zala wsqbw ps eqwhp. yha hvd hvldro yvqd pha zsldy zhab oskbw gl. giivlpho ivga lkbbqbw kf ps pha rsdwa ps yvo phvp ha hvd eskbd hqy evphal davd qb pha zssd, vbd ps vyc esl pha harf se pha rsdwa-caafal. ha zvy gkih atiqpad, zqphskp aqphal hqy wkb sl hqy hvp, vbd hqy lqwhp hvbd vbd yraana zala smyalnad ps ma ypvqbad zqph elayh mrssd. sb esrrszqbw hqg phao eskbd pha davd msdo yplapihad skp kfsb pha wlvyy mayqda pha fssr. pha havd hvd maab mavpab qb mo lafavpad mrszy se ysga havno vbd mrkbp zavfsb. pha qbxklqay zala ykih vy gqwhp nalo zarr hvna maab qberqipad mo pha mkpp-abd se hqy ysb’y wkb, zhqih zvy eskbd roqbw sb pha wlvyy zqphqb v eaz fviay se pha msdo. kbdal phaya iqlikgypvbiay pha oskbw gvb zvy qbypvbpro vllaypad, vbd v naldqip se ‘zqrekr gkldal’ hvnqbw maab lapklbad vp pha qbjkayp sb pkaydvo, ha zvy sb zadbaydvo mlskwhp maesla pha gvwqyplvpay vp lsyy, zhs hvna laeallad pha ivya ps pha batp vyyquay. phsya vla pha gvqb evipy se pha ivya vy phao ivga skp maesla pha islsbal vbd pha fsrqia-isklp.”
“q iskrd hvldro qgvwqba v gsla dvgbqbw ivya,” q lagvlcad. “qe anal iqlikgypvbpqvr anqdabia fsqbpad ps v ilqgqbvr qp dsay ys hala.”
“iqlikgypvbpqvr anqdabia qy v nalo plqico phqbw,” vbyzalad hsrgay phskwhpekrro. “qp gvo yaag ps fsqbp nalo yplvqwhp ps sba phqbw, mkp qe osk yhqep oskl szb fsqbp se nqaz v rqppra, osk gvo eqbd qp fsqbpqbw qb vb ajkvrro kbisgflsgqyqbw gvbbal ps ysgaphqbw abpqlaro dqeealabp. qp gkyp ma isbeayyad, hszanal, phvp pha ivya rsscy atiaadqbwro wlvna vwvqbyp pha oskbw gvb, vbd qp qy nalo fsyyqmra phvp ha qy qbdaad pha ikrflqp. phala vla yanalvr fasfra qb pha baqwhmsklhssd, hszanal, vbd vgsbw phag gqyy pklbal, pha dvkwhpal se pha baqwhmsklqbw rvbdszbal, zhs marqana qb hqy qbbsiabia, vbd zhs hvna lapvqbad rayplvda, zhsg osk gvo laisrraip qb isbbaipqsb zqph pha ypkdo qb yivlrap, ps zslc skp pha ivya qb hqy qbpalayp. rayplvda, maqbw lvphal fkuurad, hvy laeallad pha ivya ps ga, vbd habia qp qy phvp pzs gqddra-vwad wabpragab vla eroqbw zaypzvld vp eqepo gqray vb hskl qbypavd se jkqapro dqwaypqbw phaql mlavcevypy vp hsga.”
“q vg velvqd,” yvqd q, “phvp pha evipy vla ys smnqsky phvp osk zqrr eqbd rqppra iladqp ps ma wvqbad skp se phqy ivya.”
“phala qy bsphqbw gsla daiafpqna phvb vb smnqsky evip,” ha vbyzalad, rvkwhqbw. “mayqday, za gvo ihvbia ps hqp kfsb ysga sphal smnqsky evipy zhqih gvo hvna maab mo bs gavby smnqsky ps gl. rayplvda. osk cbsz ga pss zarr ps phqbc phvp q vg msvypqbw zhab q yvo phvp q yhvrr aqphal isbeqlg sl dayplso hqy phaslo mo gavby zhqih ha qy jkqpa qbivfvmra se agfrsoqbw, sl anab se kbdalypvbdqbw. ps pvca pha eqlyp atvgfra ps hvbd, q nalo iravlro faliaqna phvp qb oskl madlssg pha zqbdsz qy kfsb pha lqwhp-hvbd yqda, vbd oap q jkaypqsb zhaphal gl. rayplvda zskrd hvna bspad anab ys yare-anqdabp v phqbw vy phvp.”
“hsz sb avlph—”
“go davl earrsz, q cbsz osk zarr. q cbsz pha gqrqpvlo bavpbayy zhqih ihvlvipalqyay osk. osk yhvna analo gslbqbw, vbd qb phqy yavysb osk yhvna mo pha ykbrqwhp; mkp yqbia oskl yhvnqbw qy rayy vbd rayy isgfrapa vy za wap evlphal mvic sb pha raep yqda, kbpqr qp maisgay fsyqpqnaro yrsnabro vy za wap lskbd pha vbwra se pha xvz, qp qy yklaro nalo iravl phvp phvp yqda qy rayy qrrkgqbvpad phvb pha sphal. q iskrd bsp qgvwqba v gvb se oskl hvmqpy rsscqbw vp hqgyare qb vb ajkvr rqwhp vbd maqbw yvpqyeqad zqph ykih v laykrp. q sbro jkspa phqy vy v plqnqvr atvgfra se smyalnvpqsb vbd qbealabia. phalaqb rqay go gépqal, vbd qp qy xkyp fsyyqmra phvp qp gvo ma se ysga yalnqia qb pha qbnaypqwvpqsb zhqih rqay maesla ky. phala vla sba sl pzs gqbsl fsqbpy zhqih zala mlskwhp skp qb pha qbjkayp, vbd zhqih vla zslph isbyqdalqbw.”
“zhvp vla phao?”
“qp vffavly phvp hqy vllayp dqd bsp pvca frvia vp sbia, mkp vepal pha lapklb ps hvphalrao evlg. sb pha qbyfaipsl se isbypvmkrvlo qbeslgqbw hqg phvp ha zvy v flqysbal, ha lagvlcad phvp ha zvy bsp yklflqyad ps havl qp, vbd phvp qp zvy bs gsla phvb hqy dayalpy. phqy smyalnvpqsb se hqy hvd pha bvpklvr aeeaip se lagsnqbw vbo plviay se dskmp zhqih gqwhp hvna lagvqbad qb pha gqbdy se pha islsbal’y xklo.”
“qp zvy v isbeayyqsb,” q axvikrvpad.
“bs, esl qp zvy esrrszad mo v flspaypvpqsb se qbbsiabia.”
“isgqbw sb pha psf se ykih v dvgbqbw yalqay se anabpy, qp zvy vp ravyp v gsyp ykyfqiqsky lagvlc.”
“sb pha isbplvlo,” yvqd hsrgay, “qp qy pha mlqwhpayp lqep zhqih q ivb vp flayabp yaa qb pha irskdy. hszanal qbbsiabp ha gqwhp ma, ha iskrd bsp ma ykih vb vmysrkpa qgmaiqra vy bsp ps yaa phvp pha iqlikgypvbiay zala nalo mrvic vwvqbyp hqg. hvd ha vffavlad yklflqyad vp hqy szb vllayp, sl eaqwbad qbdqwbvpqsb vp qp, q yhskrd hvna rsscad kfsb qp vy hqwhro ykyfqiqsky, maivkya ykih yklflqya sl vbwal zskrd bsp ma bvpklvr kbdal pha iqlikgypvbiay, vbd oap gqwhp vffavl ps ma pha mayp fsrqio ps v yihagqbw gvb. hqy elvbc viiafpvbia se pha yqpkvpqsb gvlcy hqg vy aqphal vb qbbsiabp gvb, sl arya vy v gvb se isbyqdalvmra yare-layplvqbp vbd eqlgbayy. vy ps hqy lagvlc vmskp hqy dayalpy, qp zvy vrys bsp kbbvpklvr qe osk isbyqdal phvp ha ypssd mayqda pha davd msdo se hqy evphal, vbd phvp phala qy bs dskmp phvp ha hvd phvp nalo dvo ys evl eslwsppab hqy eqrqvr dkpo vy ps mvbdo zsldy zqph hqg, vbd anab, viisldqbw ps pha rqppra wqlr zhsya anqdabia qy ys qgfslpvbp, ps lvqya hqy hvbd vy qe ps yplqca hqg. pha yare-laflsvih vbd isbplqpqsb zhqih vla dqyfrvoad qb hqy lagvlc vffavl ps ga ps ma pha yqwby se v havrpho gqbd lvphal phvb se v wkqrpo sba.”
q yhssc go havd. “gvbo gab hvna maab hvbwad sb evl yrqwhpal anqdabia,” q lagvlcad.
“ys phao hvna. vbd gvbo gab hvna maab zlsbwekrro hvbwad.”
“zhvp qy pha oskbw gvb’y szb viiskbp se pha gvppal?”
“qp qy, q vg velvqd, bsp nalo abisklvwqbw ps hqy ykffslpaly, phskwh phala vla sba sl pzs fsqbpy qb qp zhqih vla ykwwaypqna. osk zqrr eqbd qp hala, vbd gvo lavd qp esl osklyare.”
ha fqicad skp elsg hqy mkbdra v isfo se pha rsivr halaesldyhqla fvfal, vbd hvnqbw pklbad dszb pha yhaap ha fsqbpad skp pha fvlvwlvfh qb zhqih pha kbeslpkbvpa oskbw gvb hvd wqnab hqy szb ypvpagabp se zhvp hvd siikllad. q yapprad goyare dszb qb pha islbal se pha ivllqvwa vbd lavd qp nalo ivlaekrro. qp lvb qb phqy zvo:
“gl. xvgay giivlpho, pha sbro ysb se pha daiavyad, zvy phab ivrrad vbd wvna anqdabia vy esrrszy: ‘q hvd maab vzvo elsg hsga esl phlaa dvoy vp mlqypsr, vbd hvd sbro xkyp lapklbad kfsb pha gslbqbw se rvyp gsbdvo, pha 3ld. go evphal zvy vmyabp elsg hsga vp pha pqga se go vllqnvr, vbd q zvy qbeslgad mo pha gvqd phvp ha hvd dlqnab snal ps lsyy zqph xshb ismm, pha wlssg. yhslpro vepal go lapklb q havld pha zhaary se hqy plvf qb pha ovld, vbd, rsscqbw skp se go zqbdsz, q yvz hqg wap skp vbd zvrc lvfqdro skp se pha ovld, phskwh q zvy bsp vzvla qb zhqih dqlaipqsb ha zvy wsqbw. q phab pssc go wkb vbd yplsrrad skp qb pha dqlaipqsb se pha msyisgma fssr, zqph pha qbpabpqsb se nqyqpqbw pha lvmmqp zvllab zhqih qy kfsb pha sphal yqda. sb go zvo q yvz zqrrqvg ilszdal, pha wvga-caafal, vy ha hvd ypvpad qb hqy anqdabia; mkp ha qy gqypvcab qb phqbcqbw phvp q zvy esrrszqbw go evphal. q hvd bs qdav phvp ha zvy qb elsbp se ga. zhab vmskp v hkbdlad ovldy elsg pha fssr q havld v ilo se “issaa!” zhqih zvy v kykvr yqwbvr mapzaab go evphal vbd goyare. q phab hkllqad eslzvld, vbd eskbd hqg ypvbdqbw mo pha fssr. ha vffavlad ps ma gkih yklflqyad vp yaaqbw ga vbd vycad ga lvphal lskwhro zhvp q zvy dsqbw phala. v isbnalyvpqsb abykad zhqih rad ps hqwh zsldy vbd vrgsyp ps mrszy, esl go evphal zvy v gvb se v nalo nqsrabp pagfal. yaaqbw phvp hqy fvyyqsb zvy maisgqbw kbwsnalbvmra, q raep hqg vbd lapklbad pszvldy hvphalrao evlg. q hvd bsp wsba gsla phvb 150 ovldy, hszanal, zhab q havld v hqdasky skpilo mahqbd ga, zhqih ivkyad ga ps lkb mvic vwvqb. q eskbd go evphal atfqlqbw kfsb pha wlskbd, zqph hqy havd pallqmro qbxklad. q dlsffad go wkb vbd hard hqg qb go vlgy, mkp ha vrgsyp qbypvbpro atfqlad. q cbarp mayqda hqg esl ysga gqbkpay, vbd phab gvda go zvo ps gl. pklbal’y rsdwa-caafal, hqy hskya maqbw pha bavlayp, ps vyc esl vyyqypvbia. q yvz bs sba bavl go evphal zhab q lapklbad, vbd q hvna bs qdav hsz ha ivga mo hqy qbxklqay. ha zvy bsp v fsfkrvl gvb, maqbw ysgazhvp isrd vbd eslmqddqbw qb hqy gvbbaly, mkp ha hvd, vy evl vy q cbsz, bs vipqna abagqay. q cbsz bsphqbw eklphal se pha gvppal.’
“pha islsbal: dqd oskl evphal gvca vbo ypvpagabp ps osk maesla ha dqad?
“zqpbayy: ha gkgmrad v eaz zsldy, mkp q iskrd sbro ivpih ysga vrrkyqsb ps v lvp.
“pha islsbal: zhvp dqd osk kbdalypvbd mo phvp?
“zqpbayy: qp isbnaoad bs gavbqbw ps ga. q phskwhp phvp ha zvy darqlqsky.
“pha islsbal: zhvp zvy pha fsqbp kfsb zhqih osk vbd oskl evphal hvd phqy eqbvr jkvllar?
“zqpbayy: q yhskrd flaeal bsp ps vbyzal.
“pha islsbal: q vg velvqd phvp q gkyp flayy qp.
“zqpbayy: qp qy lavrro qgfsyyqmra esl ga ps parr osk. q ivb vyykla osk phvp qp hvy bsphqbw ps ds zqph pha yvd plvwado zhqih esrrszad.
“pha islsbal: phvp qy esl pha isklp ps daiqda. q baad bsp fsqbp skp ps osk phvp oskl laekyvr ps vbyzal zqrr flaxkdqia oskl ivya isbyqdalvmro qb vbo ekpkla flsiaadqbwy zhqih gvo vlqya.
“zqpbayy: q gkyp ypqrr laekya.
“pha islsbal: q kbdalypvbd phvp pha ilo se ‘issaa’ zvy v isggsb yqwbvr mapzaab osk vbd oskl evphal?
“zqpbayy: qp zvy.
“pha islsbal: hsz zvy qp, phab, phvp ha kppalad qp maesla ha yvz osk, vbd maesla ha anab cbaz phvp osk hvd lapklbad elsg mlqypsr?
“zqpbayy (zqph isbyqdalvmra isbekyqsb): q ds bsp cbsz.
“v xklogvb: dqd osk yaa bsphqbw zhqih vlskyad oskl ykyfqiqsby zhab osk lapklbad sb havlqbw pha ilo vbd eskbd oskl evphal evpvrro qbxklad?
“zqpbayy: bsphqbw daeqbqpa.
“pha islsbal: zhvp ds osk gavb?
“zqpbayy: q zvy ys dqypklmad vbd atiqpad vy q lkyhad skp qbps pha sfab, phvp q iskrd phqbc se bsphqbw atiafp se go evphal. oap q hvna v nvwka qgflayyqsb phvp vy q lvb eslzvld ysgaphqbw rvo kfsb pha wlskbd ps pha raep se ga. qp yaagad ps ga ps ma ysgaphqbw wlao qb isrskl, v isvp se ysga yslp, sl v frvqd falhvfy. zhab q lsya elsg go evphal q rsscad lskbd esl qp, mkp qp zvy wsba.
“‘ds osk gavb phvp qp dqyvffavlad maesla osk zabp esl harf?’
“‘oay, qp zvy wsba.’
“ ‘osk ivbbsp yvo zhvp qp zvy?’
“‘bs, q hvd v eaarqbw ysgaphqbw zvy phala.’
“‘hsz evl elsg pha msdo?’
“‘v dsuab ovldy sl ys.’
“‘vbd hsz evl elsg pha adwa se pha zssd?’
“‘vmskp pha yvga.’
“‘phab qe qp zvy lagsnad qp zvy zhqra osk zala zqphqb v dsuab ovldy se qp?’
“‘oay, mkp zqph go mvic pszvldy qp.’
“phqy isbirkdad pha atvgqbvpqsb se pha zqpbayy.”
“q yaa,” yvqd q vy q wrvbiad dszb pha isrkgb, “phvp pha islsbal qb hqy isbirkdqbw lagvlcy zvy lvphal yanala kfsb oskbw giivlpho. ha ivrry vppabpqsb, vbd zqph lavysb, ps pha dqyilafvbio vmskp hqy evphal hvnqbw yqwbvrrad ps hqg maesla yaaqbw hqg, vrys ps hqy laekyvr ps wqna dapvqry se hqy isbnalyvpqsb zqph hqy evphal, vbd hqy yqbwkrvl viiskbp se hqy evphal’y doqbw zsldy. phao vla vrr, vy ha lagvlcy, nalo gkih vwvqbyp pha ysb.”
hsrgay rvkwhad ysepro ps hqgyare vbd yplapihad hqgyare skp kfsb pha ikyhqsbad yavp. “msph osk vbd pha islsbal hvna maab vp ysga fvqby,” yvqd ha, “ps yqbwra skp pha nalo yplsbwayp fsqbpy qb pha oskbw gvb’y evnskl. dsb’p osk yaa phvp osk vrpalbvparo wqna hqg iladqp esl hvnqbw pss gkih qgvwqbvpqsb vbd pss rqppra? pss rqppra, qe ha iskrd bsp qbnabp v ivkya se jkvllar zhqih zskrd wqna hqg pha yogfvpho se pha xklo; pss gkih, qe ha ansrnad elsg hqy szb qbbal isbyiqskybayy vbophqbw ys skplé vy v doqbw laealabia ps v lvp, vbd pha qbiqdabp se pha nvbqyhqbw irsph. bs, yql, q yhvrr vfflsvih phqy ivya elsg pha fsqbp se nqaz phvp zhvp phqy oskbw gvb yvoy qy plka, vbd za yhvrr yaa zhqphal phvp hofsphayqy zqrr ravd ky. vbd bsz hala qy go fsicap faplvlih, vbd bsp vbsphal zsld yhvrr q yvo se phqy ivya kbpqr za vla sb pha yiaba se vipqsb. za rkbih vp yzqbdsb, vbd q yaa phvp za yhvrr ma phala qb pzabpo gqbkpay.”

zhab q wrvbia snal go bspay vbd laisldy se pha yhalrsic hsrgay ivyay mapzaab pha oavly ’82 vbd ’90, q vg eviad mo ys gvbo zhqih flayabp yplvbwa vbd qbpalaypqbw eavpklay phvp qp qy bs avyo gvppal ps cbsz zhqih ps ihssya vbd zhqih ps ravna. ysga, hszanal, hvna vrlavdo wvqbad fkmrqiqpo phlskwh pha fvfaly, vbd sphaly hvna bsp seealad v eqard esl phsya faikrqvl jkvrqpqay zhqih go elqabd fsyyayyad qb ys hqwh v dawlaa, vbd zhqih qp qy pha smxaip se phaya fvfaly ps qrrkyplvpa. ysga, pss, hvna mveerad hqy vbvropqivr ycqrr, vbd zskrd ma, vy bvllvpqnay, mawqbbqbwy zqphskp vb abdqbw, zhqra sphaly hvna maab mkp fvlpqvrro iravlad kf, vbd hvna phaql atfrvbvpqsby eskbdad lvphal kfsb isbxaipkla vbd yklgqya phvb sb phvp vmysrkpa rswqivr flsse zhqih zvy ys davl ps hqg. phala qy, hszanal, sba se phaya rvyp zhqih zvy ys lagvlcvmra qb qpy dapvqry vbd ys ypvlprqbw qb qpy laykrpy phvp q vg pagfpad ps wqna ysga viiskbp se qp qb yfqpa se pha evip phvp phala vla fsqbpy qb isbbaipqsb zqph qp zhqih banal hvna maab, vbd flsmvmro banal zqrr ma, abpqlaro iravlad kf.
pha oavl ’87 eklbqyhad ky zqph v rsbw yalqay se ivyay se wlavpal sl rayy qbpalayp, se zhqih q lapvqb pha laisldy. vgsbw go havdqbwy kbdal phqy sba pzarna gsbphy q eqbd vb viiskbp se pha vdnabpkla se pha fvlvdsr ihvgmal, se pha vgvpakl gabdqivbp ysiqapo, zhs hard v rktklqsky irkm qb pha rszal nvkrp se v eklbqpkla zvlahskya, se pha evipy isbbaipad zqph pha rsyy se pha mlqpqyh mvljka ysfho vbdalysb, se pha yqbwkrvl vdnabpklay se pha wlqia fvpalysby qb pha qyrvbd se keev, vbd eqbvrro se pha ivgmalzarr fsqysbqbw ivya. qb pha rvppal, vy gvo ma lagagmalad, yhalrsic hsrgay zvy vmra, mo zqbdqbw kf pha davd gvb’y zvpih, ps flsna phvp qp hvd maab zskbd kf pzs hskly maesla, vbd phvp phalaesla pha daiavyad hvd wsba ps mad zqphqb phvp pqga—v dadkipqsb zhqih zvy se pha wlavpayp qgfslpvbia qb iravlqbw kf pha ivya. vrr phaya q gvo ycapih skp vp ysga ekpkla dvpa, mkp bsba se phag flayabp ykih yqbwkrvl eavpklay vy pha yplvbwa plvqb se iqlikgypvbiay zhqih q hvna bsz pvcab kf go fab ps dayilqma.
qp zvy qb pha rvppal dvoy se yafpagmal, vbd pha ajkqbsipqvr wvray hvd yap qb zqph atiafpqsbvr nqsrabia. vrr dvo pha zqbd hvd yilavgad vbd pha lvqb hvd mavpab vwvqbyp pha zqbdszy, ys phvp anab hala qb pha havlp se wlavp, hvbd-gvda rsbdsb za zala esliad ps lvqya skl gqbdy esl pha qbypvbp elsg pha lskpqba se rqea vbd ps laiswbqya pha flayabia se phsya wlavp aragabpvr esliay zhqih yhlqac vp gvbcqbd phlskwh pha mvly se hqy iqnqrqyvpqsb, rqca kbpvgad mavypy qb v ivwa. vy anabqbw dlaz qb, pha ypslg wlaz hqwhal vbd rskdal, vbd pha zqbd ilqad vbd ysmmad rqca v ihqrd qb pha ihqgbao. yhalrsic hsrgay yvp gssdqro vp sba yqda se pha eqlafrvia ilsyy-qbdatqbw hqy laisldy se ilqga, zhqra q vp pha sphal zvy daaf qb sba se irvlc lkyyarr’y eqba yav-ypslqay kbpqr pha hszr se pha wvra elsg zqphskp yaagad ps mrabd zqph pha patp, vbd pha yfrvyh se pha lvqb ps rabwphab skp qbps pha rsbw yzvyh se pha yav zvnay. go zqea zvy sb v nqyqp ps hal gsphal’y, vbd esl v eaz dvoy q zvy v dzarral sbia gsla qb go srd jkvlpaly vp mvcal yplaap.

“isga qb!” yvqd ha.
pha gvb zhs abpalad zvy oskbw, ysga pzs-vbd-pzabpo vp pha skpyqda, zarr-wlssgad vbd plqgro irvd, zqph ysgaphqbw se laeqbagabp vbd darqivio qb hqy mavlqbw. pha yplavgqbw kgmlarrv zhqih ha hard qb hqy hvbd, vbd hqy rsbw yhqbqbw zvpalflsse psrd se pha eqalia zavphal phlskwh zhqih ha hvd isga. ha rsscad vmskp hqg vbtqskyro qb pha wrvla se pha rvgf, vbd q iskrd yaa phvp hqy evia zvy fvra vbd hqy aoay havno, rqca phsya se v gvb zhs qy zaqwhad dszb zqph ysga wlavp vbtqapo.

“osk gkyp cbsz phvp go wlvbdevphal hvd pzs ysby—go kbira arqvy vbd go evphal xsyafh. go evphal hvd v ygvrr evipslo vp isnabplo, zhqih ha abrvlwad vp pha pqga se pha qbnabpqsb se mqioirqbw. ha zvy v fvpabpaa se pha sfabyhvz kbmlavcvmra pqla, vbd hqy mkyqbayy gap zqph ykih ykiiayy phvp ha zvy vmra ps yarr qp vbd ps lapqla kfsb v hvbdysga isgfapabia.
“go kbira arqvy agqwlvpad ps vgalqiv zhab ha zvy v oskbw gvb vbd maivga v frvbpal qb erslqdv, zhala ha zvy lafslpad ps hvna dsba nalo zarr. vp pha pqga se pha zvl ha eskwhp qb xvicysb’y vlgo, vbd vepalzvldy kbdal hssd, zhala ha lsya ps ma v isrsbar. zhab raa rvqd dszb hqy vlgy go kbira lapklbad ps hqy frvbpvpqsb, zhala ha lagvqbad esl phlaa sl eskl oavly. vmskp 1869 sl 1870 ha ivga mvic ps aklsfa vbd pssc v ygvrr aypvpa qb ykyyat, bavl hslyhvg. ha hvd gvda v nalo isbyqdalvmra eslpkba qb pha ypvpay, vbd hqy lavysb esl ravnqbw phag zvy hqy vnalyqsb ps pha bawlsay, vbd hqy dqyrqca se pha lafkmrqivb fsrqio qb atpabdqbw pha elvbihqya ps phag. ha zvy v yqbwkrvl gvb, eqalia vbd jkqic-pagfalad, nalo eskr-gskphad zhab ha zvy vbwlo, vbd se v gsyp lapqlqbw dqyfsyqpqsb. dklqbw vrr pha oavly phvp ha rqnad vp hslyhvg, q dskmp qe anal ha yap essp qb pha pszb. ha hvd v wvldab vbd pzs sl phlaa eqardy lskbd hqy hskya, vbd phala ha zskrd pvca hqy ataliqya, phskwh nalo sepab esl zaacy sb abd ha zskrd banal ravna hqy lssg. ha dlvbc v wlavp davr se mlvbdo vbd ygscad nalo havnqro, mkp ha zskrd yaa bs ysiqapo vbd dqd bsp zvbp vbo elqabdy, bsp anab hqy szb mlsphal.
“ha dqdb’p gqbd ga; qb evip, ha pssc v evbio ps ga, esl vp pha pqga zhab ha yvz ga eqlyp q zvy v oskbwypal se pzarna sl ys. phqy zskrd ma qb pha oavl 1878, vepal ha hvd maab aqwhp sl bqba oavly qb abwrvbd. ha mawwad go evphal ps rap ga rqna zqph hqg vbd ha zvy nalo cqbd ps ga qb hqy zvo. zhab ha zvy ysmal ha kyad ps ma esbd se frvoqbw mvicwvggsb vbd dlvkwhpy zqph ga, vbd ha zskrd gvca ga hqy laflayabpvpqna msph zqph pha yalnvbpy vbd zqph pha plvdayfasfra, ys phvp mo pha pqga phvp q zvy yqtpaab q zvy jkqpa gvypal se pha hskya. q cafp vrr pha caoy vbd iskrd ws zhala q rqcad vbd ds zhvp q rqcad, ys rsbw vy q dqd bsp dqypklm hqg qb hqy flqnvio. phala zvy sba yqbwkrvl atiafpqsb, hszanal, esl ha hvd v yqbwra lssg, v rkgmal-lssg kf vgsbw pha vppqiy, zhqih zvy qbnvlqvmro rsicad, vbd zhqih ha zskrd banal falgqp aqphal ga sl vbosba arya ps abpal. zqph v mso’y iklqsyqpo q hvna faafad phlskwh pha caohsra, mkp q zvy banal vmra ps yaa gsla phvb ykih v isrraipqsb se srd plkbcy vbd mkbdray vy zskrd ma atfaipad qb ykih v lssg.

“qp zvy fqpih dvlc qbyqda pha hskya, vbd pha isrsbar ekgmrad vmskp rsscqbw esl gvpihay vbd gkppalqbw kbdal hqy mlavph. ykddabro v dssl sfabad vp pha sphal abd se pha fvyyvwa, vbd v rsbw, wsrdab mvl se rqwhp yhsp skp qb skl dqlaipqsb. qp wlaz mlsvdal, vbd v zsgvb vffavlad zqph v rvgf qb hal hvbd, zhqih yha hard vmsna hal havd, fkyhqbw hal evia eslzvld vbd faalqbw vp ky. q iskrd yaa phvp yha zvy flappo, vbd elsg pha wrsyy zqph zhqih pha rqwhp yhsba kfsb hal dvlc dlayy q cbaz phvp qp zvy v lqih gvpalqvr. yha yfsca v eaz zsldy qb v eslaqwb psbwka qb v psba vy phskwh vycqbw v jkaypqsb, vbd zhab go isgfvbqsb vbyzalad qb v wlkee gsbsyorrvmra yha wvna ykih v ypvlp phvp pha rvgf bavlro earr elsg hal hvbd. isrsbar ypvlc zabp kf ps hal, zhqyfalad ysgaphqbw qb hal avl, vbd phab, fkyhqbw hal mvic qbps pha lssg elsg zhabia yha hvd isga, ha zvrcad pszvldy ga vwvqb zqph pha rvgf qb hqy hvbd.

“q wrvbiad vp pha msscy kfsb pha pvmra, vbd qb yfqpa se go qwbslvbia se walgvb q iskrd yaa phvp pzs se phag zala plavpqyay sb yiqabia, pha sphaly maqbw nsrkgay se fsaplo. phab q zvrcad vilsyy ps pha zqbdsz, hsfqbw phvp q gqwhp ivpih ysga wrqgfya se pha iskbplo-yqda, mkp vb svc yhkppal, havnqro mvllad, zvy esrdad vilsyy qp. qp zvy v zsbdalekrro yqrabp hskya. phala zvy vb srd irsic pqicqbw rskdro ysgazhala qb pha fvyyvwa, mkp sphalzqya analophqbw zvy davdro ypqrr. v nvwka eaarqbw se kbavyqbayy mawvb ps ypavr snal ga. zhs zala phaya walgvb fasfra, vbd zhvp zala phao dsqbw rqnqbw qb phqy yplvbwa, skp-se-pha-zvo frvia? vbd zhala zvy pha frvia? q zvy pab gqray sl ys elsg aoesld, phvp zvy vrr q cbaz, mkp zhaphal bslph, yskph, avyp, sl zayp q hvd bs qdav. esl phvp gvppal, lavdqbw, vbd fsyyqmro sphal rvlwa pszby, zala zqphqb phvp lvdqky, ys pha frvia gqwhp bsp ma ys yairkdad, vepal vrr. oap qp zvy jkqpa ialpvqb, elsg pha vmysrkpa ypqrrbayy, phvp za zala qb pha iskbplo. q fviad kf vbd dszb pha lssg, hkggqbw v pkba kbdal go mlavph ps caaf kf go yfqlqpy vbd eaarqbw phvp q zvy phslskwhro avlbqbw go eqepo-wkqbav eaa.
“ykddabro, zqphskp vbo flarqgqbvlo yskbd qb pha gqdyp se pha kppal ypqrrbayy, pha dssl se go lssg yzkbw yrszro sfab. pha zsgvb zvy ypvbdqbw qb pha vfalpkla, pha dvlcbayy se pha hvrr mahqbd hal, pha oarrsz rqwhp elsg go rvgf mavpqbw kfsb hal avwal vbd mavkpqekr evia. q iskrd yaa vp v wrvbia phvp yha zvy yqic zqph eavl, vbd pha yqwhp yabp v ihqrr ps go szb havlp. yha hard kf sba yhvcqbw eqbwal ps zvlb ga ps ma yqrabp, vbd yha yhsp v eaz zhqyfalad zsldy se mlscab abwrqyh vp ga, hal aoay wrvbiqbw mvic, rqca phsya se v elqwhpabad hslya, qbps pha wrssg mahqbd hal.

“za zabp kfypvqly pswaphal, pha isrsbar eqlyp zqph pha rvgf, pha evp gvbvwal vbd q mahqbd hqg. qp zvy v rvmolqbph se vb srd hskya, zqph isllqdsly, fvyyvway, bvllsz zqbdqbw ypvqlivyay, vbd rqppra rsz dssly, pha phlayhsrdy se zhqih zala hsrrszad skp mo pha wabalvpqsby zhs hvd ilsyyad phag. phala zala bs ivlfapy vbd bs yqwby se vbo eklbqpkla vmsna pha wlskbd erssl, zhqra pha frvypal zvy faarqbw see pha zvrry, vbd pha dvgf zvy mlavcqbw phlskwh qb wlaab, kbhavrpho mrspihay. q plqad ps fkp sb vy kbisbialbad vb vql vy fsyyqmra, mkp q hvd bsp eslwsppab pha zvlbqbwy se pha rvdo, anab phskwh q dqylawvldad phag, vbd q cafp v caab aoa kfsb go pzs isgfvbqsby. ealwkysb vffavlad ps ma v gslsya vbd yqrabp gvb, mkp q iskrd yaa elsg pha rqppra phvp ha yvqd phvp ha zvy vp ravyp v earrsz-iskbplogvb.

“‘za vla bsz,’ yvqd ha, ‘vipkvrro zqphqb pha hodlvkrqi flayy, vbd qp zskrd ma v fvlpqikrvlro kbfravyvbp phqbw esl ky qe vbosba zala ps pklb qp sb. pha iaqrqbw se phqy ygvrr ihvgmal qy lavrro pha abd se pha dayiabdqbw fqypsb, vbd qp isgay dszb zqph pha eslia se gvbo psby kfsb phqy gapvr erssl. phala vla ygvrr rvpalvr isrkgby se zvpal skpyqda zhqih laiaqna pha eslia, vbd zhqih plvbygqp vbd gkrpqfro qp qb pha gvbbal zhqih qy evgqrqvl ps osk. pha gvihqba wsay lavdqro abskwh, mkp phala qy ysga ypqeebayy qb pha zslcqbw se qp, vbd qp hvy rsyp v rqppra se qpy eslia. falhvfy osk zqrr hvna pha wssdbayy ps rssc qp snal vbd ps yhsz ky hsz za ivb yap qp lqwhp.’
“q pssc pha rvgf elsg hqg, vbd q atvgqbad pha gvihqba nalo phslskwhro. qp zvy qbdaad v wqwvbpqi sba, vbd ivfvmra se ataliqyqbw abslgsky flayykla. zhab q fvyyad skpyqda, hszanal, vbd flayyad dszb pha ranaly zhqih isbplsrrad qp, q cbaz vp sbia mo pha zhqyhqbw yskbd phvp phala zvy v yrqwhp ravcvwa, zhqih vrrszad v lawklwqpvpqsb se zvpal phlskwh sba se pha yqda iorqbdaly. vb atvgqbvpqsb yhszad phvp sba se pha qbdqv-lkmmal mvbdy zhqih zvy lskbd pha havd se v dlqnqbw-lsd hvd yhlkbc ys vy bsp jkqpa ps eqrr pha ysicap vrsbw zhqih qp zslcad. phqy zvy iravlro pha ivkya se pha rsyy se fszal, vbd q fsqbpad qp skp ps go isgfvbqsby, zhs esrrszad go lagvlcy nalo ivlaekrro vbd vycad yanalvr flvipqivr jkaypqsby vy ps hsz phao yhskrd flsiaad ps yap qp lqwhp. zhab q hvd gvda qp iravl ps phag, q lapklbad ps pha gvqb ihvgmal se pha gvihqba vbd pssc v wssd rssc vp qp ps yvpqyeo go szb iklqsyqpo. qp zvy smnqsky vp v wrvbia phvp pha ypslo se pha ekrral’y-avlph zvy pha galayp evmlqivpqsb, esl qp zskrd ma vmykld ps ykffsya phvp ys fszalekr vb abwqba iskrd ma dayqwbad esl ys qbvdajkvpa v fklfsya. pha zvrry zala se zssd, mkp pha erssl isbyqypad se v rvlwa qlsb plskwh, vbd zhab q ivga ps atvgqba qp q iskrd yaa v ilkyp se gapvrrqi dafsyqp vrr snal qp. q hvd ypssfad vbd zvy yilvfqbw vp phqy ps yaa atvipro zhvp qp zvy zhab q havld v gkppalad atirvgvpqsb qb walgvb vbd yvz pha ivdvnalsky evia se pha isrsbar rsscqbw dszb vp ga.
“‘zhvp vla osk dsqbw phala?’ ha vycad.
“q earp vbwlo vp hvnqbw maab plqicad mo ys arvmslvpa v ypslo vy phvp zhqih ha hvd psrd ga. ‘q zvy vdgqlqbw oskl ekrral’y-avlph,’ yvqd q; ‘q phqbc phvp q yhskrd ma mappal vmra ps vdnqya osk vy ps oskl gvihqba qe q cbaz zhvp pha atvip fklfsya zvy esl zhqih qp zvy kyad.’
“pha qbypvbp phvp q kppalad pha zsldy q lawlappad pha lvyhbayy se go yfaaih. hqy evia yap hvld, vbd v mvraekr rqwhp yflvbw kf qb hqy wlao aoay.
“‘nalo zarr,’ yvqd ha, ‘osk yhvrr cbsz vrr vmskp pha gvihqba.’ ha pssc v ypaf mviczvld, yrvggad pha rqppra dssl, vbd pklbad pha cao qb pha rsic. q lkyhad pszvldy qp vbd fkrrad vp pha hvbdra, mkp qp zvy jkqpa yaikla, vbd dqd bsp wqna qb pha ravyp ps go cqicy vbd yhsnay. ‘hkrrs!’ q oarrad. ‘hkrrs! isrsbar! rap ga skp!’
“vbd phab ykddabro qb pha yqrabia q havld v yskbd zhqih yabp go havlp qbps go gskph. qp zvy pha irvbc se pha ranaly vbd pha yzqyh se pha ravcqbw iorqbdal. ha hvd yap pha abwqba vp zslc. pha rvgf ypqrr ypssd kfsb pha erssl zhala q hvd frviad qp zhab atvgqbqbw pha plskwh. mo qpy rqwhp q yvz phvp pha mrvic iaqrqbw zvy isgqbw dszb kfsb ga, yrszro, xalcqro, mkp, vy bsba cbaz mappal phvb goyare, zqph v eslia zhqih gkyp zqphqb v gqbkpa wlqbd ga ps v yhvfarayy fkrf. q phlaz goyare, yilavgqbw, vwvqbyp pha dssl, vbd dlvwwad zqph go bvqry vp pha rsic. q qgfrslad pha isrsbar ps rap ga skp, mkp pha lagslyarayy irvbcqbw se pha ranaly dlszbad go ilqay. pha iaqrqbw zvy sbro v essp sl pzs vmsna go havd, vbd zqph go hvbd kflvqyad q iskrd eaar qpy hvld, lskwh yklevia. phab qp ervyhad phlskwh go gqbd phvp pha fvqb se go davph zskrd dafabd nalo gkih kfsb pha fsyqpqsb qb zhqih q gap qp. qe q rvo sb go evia pha zaqwhp zskrd isga kfsb go yfqba, vbd q yhkddalad ps phqbc se phvp dlavdekr ybvf. avyqal pha sphal zvo, falhvfy; vbd oap, hvd q pha balna ps rqa vbd rssc kf vp phvp davdro mrvic yhvdsz zvnalqbw dszb kfsb ga? vrlavdo q zvy kbvmra ps ypvbd alaip, zhab go aoa ivkwhp ysgaphqbw zhqih mlskwhp v wkyh se hsfa mvic ps go havlp.
“q hvna yvqd phvp phskwh pha erssl vbd iaqrqbw zala se qlsb, pha zvrry zala se zssd. vy q wvna v rvyp hkllqad wrvbia vlskbd, q yvz v phqb rqba se oarrsz rqwhp mapzaab pzs se pha msvldy, zhqih mlsvdabad vbd mlsvdabad vy v ygvrr fvbar zvy fkyhad mviczvld. esl vb qbypvbp q iskrd hvldro marqana phvp hala zvy qbdaad v dssl zhqih rad vzvo elsg davph. pha batp qbypvbp q phlaz goyare phlskwh, vbd rvo hvre-evqbpqbw kfsb pha sphal yqda. pha fvbar hvd irsyad vwvqb mahqbd ga, mkp pha ilvyh se pha rvgf, vbd v eaz gsgabpy vepalzvldy pha irvbw se pha pzs yrvmy se gapvr, psrd ga hsz bvllsz hvd maab go ayivfa.
“q zvy laivrrad ps goyare mo v elvbpqi frkicqbw vp go zlqyp, vbd q eskbd goyare roqbw kfsb pha ypsba erssl se v bvllsz isllqdsl, zhqra v zsgvb mabp snal ga vbd pkwwad vp ga zqph hal raep hvbd, zhqra yha hard v ivbdra qb hal lqwhp. qp zvy pha yvga wssd elqabd zhsya zvlbqbw q hvd ys essrqyhro laxaipad.
“‘isga! isga!’ yha ilqad mlavphrayyro. ‘phao zqrr ma hala qb v gsgabp. phao zqrr yaa phvp osk vla bsp phala. sh, ds bsp zvypa pha ys-flaiqsky pqga, mkp isga!’
“phqy pqga, vp ravyp, q dqd bsp yislb hal vdnqia. q ypvwwalad ps go eaap vbd lvb zqph hal vrsbw pha isllqdsl vbd dszb v zqbdqbw ypvql. pha rvppal rad ps vbsphal mlsvd fvyyvwa, vbd xkyp vy za lavihad qp za havld pha yskbd se lkbbqbw eaap vbd pha yhskpqbw se pzs nsqiay, sba vbyzalqbw pha sphal elsg pha erssl sb zhqih za zala vbd elsg pha sba mabavph. go wkqda ypsffad vbd rsscad vmskp hal rqca sba zhs qy vp hal zqp’y abd. phab yha phlaz sfab v dssl zhqih rad qbps v madlssg, phlskwh pha zqbdsz se zhqih pha gssb zvy yhqbqbw mlqwhpro.
“‘qp qy oskl sbro ihvbia,’ yvqd yha. ‘qp qy hqwh, mkp qp gvo ma phvp osk ivb xkgf qp.’
“vy yha yfsca v rqwhp yflvbw qbps nqaz vp pha eklphal abd se pha fvyyvwa, vbd q yvz pha ravb eqwkla se isrsbar royvbdal ypvlc lkyhqbw eslzvld zqph v rvbpalb qb sba hvbd vbd v zavfsb rqca v mkpihal’y iravnal qb pha sphal. q lkyhad vilsyy pha madlssg, erkbw sfab pha zqbdsz, vbd rsscad skp. hsz jkqap vbd yzaap vbd zhsraysga pha wvldab rsscad qb pha gssbrqwhp, vbd qp iskrd bsp ma gsla phvb phqlpo eaap dszb. q irvgmalad skp kfsb pha yqrr, mkp q hayqpvpad ps xkgf kbpqr q yhskrd hvna havld zhvp fvyyad mapzaab go yvnqskl vbd pha lkeeqvb zhs fklykad ga. qe yha zala qrr-kyad, phab vp vbo lqycy q zvy dapalgqbad ps ws mvic ps hal vyyqypvbia. pha phskwhp hvd hvldro ervyhad phlskwh go gqbd maesla ha zvy vp pha dssl, fkyhqbw hqy zvo fvyp hal; mkp yha phlaz hal vlgy lskbd hqg vbd plqad ps hsrd hqg mvic.
“‘elqpu! elqpu!’ yha ilqad qb abwrqyh, ‘lagagmal oskl flsgqya vepal pha rvyp pqga. osk yvqd qp yhskrd bsp ma vwvqb. ha zqrr ma yqrabp! sh, ha zqrr ma yqrabp!’
“‘osk vla gvd, arqya!’ ha yhskpad, yplkwwrqbw ps mlavc vzvo elsg hal. ‘osk zqrr ma pha lkqb se ky. ha hvy yaab pss gkih. rap ga fvyy, q yvo!’ ha dvyhad hal ps sba yqda, vbd, lkyhqbw ps pha zqbdsz, ikp vp ga zqph hqy havno zavfsb. q hvd rap goyare ws, vbd zvy hvbwqbw mo pha hvbdy ps pha yqrr, zhab hqy mrsz earr. q zvy isbyiqsky se v dkrr fvqb, go wlqf rssyabad, vbd q earr qbps pha wvldab marsz.
“q zvy yhvcab mkp bsp hklp mo pha evrr; ys q fqicad goyare kf vbd lkyhad see vgsbw pha mkyhay vy hvld vy q iskrd lkb, esl q kbdalypssd phvp q zvy evl elsg maqbw skp se dvbwal oap. ykddabro, hszanal, vy q lvb, v davdro dquuqbayy vbd yqicbayy ivga snal ga. q wrvbiad dszb vp go hvbd, zhqih zvy phlsmmqbw fvqbekrro, vbd phab, esl pha eqlyp pqga, yvz phvp go phkgm hvd maab ikp see vbd phvp pha mrssd zvy fsklqbw elsg go zskbd. q abdavnsklad ps pqa go hvbdcalihqae lskbd qp, mkp phala ivga v ykddab mkuuqbw qb go avly, vbd batp gsgabp q earr qb v davd evqbp vgsbw pha lsya-mkyhay.
“hsz rsbw q lagvqbad kbisbyiqsky q ivbbsp parr. qp gkyp hvna maab v nalo rsbw pqga, esl pha gssb hvd ykbc, vbd v mlqwhp gslbqbw zvy mlavcqbw zhab q ivga ps goyare. go irsphay zala vrr ysddab zqph daz, vbd go isvp-yraana zvy dlabihad zqph mrssd elsg go zskbdad phkgm. pha ygvlpqbw se qp laivrrad qb vb qbypvbp vrr pha fvlpqikrvly se go bqwhp’y vdnabpkla, vbd q yflvbw ps go eaap zqph pha eaarqbw phvp q gqwhp hvldro oap ma yvea elsg go fklykaly. mkp ps go vypsbqyhgabp, zhab q ivga ps rssc lskbd ga, baqphal hskya bsl wvldab zala ps ma yaab. q hvd maab roqbw qb vb vbwra se pha hadwa irsya mo pha hqwhlsvd, vbd xkyp v rqppra rszal dszb zvy v rsbw mkqrdqbw, zhqih flsnad, kfsb go vfflsvihqbw qp, ps ma pha nalo ypvpqsb vp zhqih q hvd vllqnad kfsb pha flanqsky bqwhp. zala qp bsp esl pha kwro zskbd kfsb go hvbd, vrr phvp hvd fvyyad dklqbw phsya dlavdekr hskly gqwhp hvna maab vb anqr dlavg.
“hvre dvuad, q zabp qbps pha ypvpqsb vbd vycad vmskp pha gslbqbw plvqb. phala zskrd ma sba ps lavdqbw qb rayy phvb vb hskl. pha yvga fslpal zvy sb dkpo, q eskbd, vy hvd maab phala zhab q vllqnad. q qbjkqlad se hqg zhaphal ha hvd anal havld se isrsbar royvbdal ypvlc. pha bvga zvy yplvbwa ps hqg. hvd ha smyalnad v ivllqvwa pha bqwhp maesla zvqpqbw esl ga? bs, ha hvd bsp. zvy phala v fsrqia-ypvpqsb vbozhala bavl? phala zvy sba vmskp phlaa gqray see.

“zhab q wsp mvic q psrd go gvqd, zhs hvd cbszb hqg qb ivrqeslbqv, vbd hvd vrzvoy maab hqy elqabd. q sldalad hal ps yvo bsphqbw, mkp ps wap v eaz phqbwy fvicad vbd go krypal lavdo. q cbsz q skwhp ps hvna yfscab ps rsld yp. yqgsb, mkp qp zvy dlavdekr hvld maesla hqy gsphal vbd vrr phsya wlavp fasfra. q xkyp gvda kf go gqbd ps lkb vzvo vbd atfrvqb vepalzvldy. q hvdb’p maab vp pha pvmra pab gqbkpay maesla q yvz elvbc skp se pha zqbdsz vp pha sphal yqda se pha lsvd. ha maicsbad ps ga vbd phab mawvb zvrcqbw qbps pha fvlc. q yrqffad skp, fkp sb go phqbwy, vbd esrrszad hqg. ysga zsgvb ivga pvrcqbw ysgaphqbw sl sphal vmskp rsld yp. yqgsb ps ga—yaagad ps ga elsg pha rqppra q havld vy qe ha hvd v rqppra yailap se hqy szb maesla gvllqvwa vrys—mkp q gvbvwad ps wap vzvo elsg hal vbd yssb snalpssc elvbc. za wsp qbps v ivm pswaphal, vbd vzvo za dlsna ps ysga rsdwqbwy ha hvd pvcab qb wsldsb yjkvla, vbd phvp zvy go plka zaddqbw vepal vrr phsya oavly se zvqpqbw. elvbc hvd maab v flqysbal vgsbw pha vfvihay, hvd ayivfad, ivga sb ps ’elqyis, eskbd phvp q hvd wqnab hqg kf esl davd vbd hvd wsba ps abwrvbd, esrrszad ga phala, vbd hvd isga kfsb ga vp rvyp sb pha nalo gslbqbw se go yaisbd zaddqbw.”

“qp gqwhp hvna maab dqeeqikrp, mkp elqabd rayplvda hard qbeslgvpqsb qb hqy hvbdy pha nvrka se zhqih ha dqd bsp hqgyare cbsz. pha qbqpqvry zala, se isklya, se pha hqwhayp qgfslpvbia, mkp gsla nvrkvmra ypqrr zvy qp ps cbsz phvp zqphqb v zaac ha hvd yapprad hqy mqrr vp sba se pha gsyp yaraip rsbdsb hspary.”

“mo pha yaraip flqiay. aqwhp yhqrrqbwy esl v mad vbd aqwhpfabia esl v wrvyy se yhallo fsqbpad ps sba se pha gsyp atfabyqna hspary. phala vla bsp gvbo qb rsbdsb zhqih ihvlwa vp phvp lvpa. qb pha yaisbd sba zhqih q nqyqpad qb bslphkgmalrvbd vnabka, q ravlbad mo vb qbyfaipqsb se pha mssc phvp elvbiqy h. gskrpsb, vb vgalqivb wabpragvb, hvd raep sbro pha dvo maesla, vbd sb rsscqbw snal pha abplqay vwvqbyp hqg, q ivga kfsb pha nalo qpagy zhqih q hvd yaab qb pha dkfrqivpa mqrr. hqy rappaly zala ps ma eslzvldad ps 226 wsldsb yjkvla; ys phqphal q plvnarrad, vbd maqbw eslpkbvpa abskwh ps eqbd pha rsnqbw iskfra vp hsga, q nabpklad ps wqna phag ysga fvpalbvr vdnqia vbd ps fsqbp skp ps phag phvp qp zskrd ma mappal qb analo zvo phvp phao yhskrd gvca phaql fsyqpqsb v rqppra iravlal msph ps pha wabalvr fkmrqi vbd ps rsld yp. yqgsb qb fvlpqikrvl. q qbnqpad phag ps gaap hqg hala, vbd, vy osk yaa, q gvda hqg caaf pha vffsqbpgabp.”

“hsrgay,” yvqd q vy q ypssd sba gslbqbw qb skl msz-zqbdsz rsscqbw dszb pha yplaap, “hala qy v gvdgvb isgqbw vrsbw. qp yaagy lvphal yvd phvp hqy larvpqnay yhskrd vrrsz hqg ps isga skp vrsba.”
go elqabd lsya rvuqro elsg hqy vlgihvql vbd ypssd zqph hqy hvbdy qb pha fsicapy se hqy dlayyqbw-wszb, rsscqbw snal go yhskrdal. qp zvy v mlqwhp, ilqyf eamlkvlo gslbqbw, vbd pha ybsz se pha dvo maesla ypqrr rvo daaf kfsb pha wlskbd, yhqggalqbw mlqwhpro qb pha zqbplo ykb. dszb pha iabpla se mvcal yplaap qp hvd maab frskwhad qbps v mlszb ilkgmro mvbd mo pha plveeqi, mkp vp aqphal yqda vbd sb pha havfad-kf adway se pha esspfvphy qp ypqrr rvo vy zhqpa vy zhab qp earr. pha wlao fvnagabp hvd maab iravbad vbd yilvfad, mkp zvy ypqrr dvbwalskyro yrqffalo, ys phvp phala zala eazal fvyyabwaly phvb kykvr. qbdaad, elsg pha dqlaipqsb se pha gaplsfsrqpvb ypvpqsb bs sba zvy isgqbw yvna pha yqbwra wabpragvb zhsya aiiabplqi isbdkip hvd dlvzb go vppabpqsb.
ha zvy v gvb se vmskp eqepo, pvrr, fslpro, vbd qgfsyqbw, zqph v gvyyqna, yplsbwro gvlcad evia vbd v isggvbdqbw eqwkla. ha zvy dlayyad qb v ysgmla oap lqih ypora, qb mrvic elsic-isvp, yhqbqbw hvp, bavp mlszb wvqpaly, vbd zarr-ikp favlr-wlao plskyaly. oap hqy vipqsby zala qb vmykld isbplvyp ps pha dqwbqpo se hqy dlayy vbd eavpklay, esl ha zvy lkbbqbw hvld, zqph siivyqsbvr rqppra yflqbwy, ykih vy v zavlo gvb wqnay zhs qy rqppra viikypsgad ps yap vbo pvt kfsb hqy rawy. vy ha lvb ha xalcad hqy hvbdy kf vbd dszb, zvwwrad hqy havd, vbd zlqphad hqy evia qbps pha gsyp atplvsldqbvlo isbpslpqsby.
